# GROWTH Narrative Map

> Consolidated narrative canon map of Michael "Mike" Kantack's GROWTH universe, extracted 2026-07-06 → 2026-07-08 from all available sources.
> **Nothing here is invented.** Gaps are marked `UNKNOWN — needs Michael`; deductions are labeled `[inferred]`;
> lore that only ever appeared in AI replies (never confirmed by Mike) is tagged `[AI-proposed — adoption unknown]`.
> Rulings needed: see **CONTRADICTIONS** (C-1…C-41; C-1…C-15 ruled 2026-07-09) and **OPEN QUESTIONS** (Q-1…Q-140; 14 annotated answered/partial 2026-07-09).

## Method & Coverage

| Source | Scanned | Used |
|---|---|---|
| Claude export (conversations.json) | 385 conversations | 240 GROWTH-relevant |
| ChatGPT export (19 shards) | 1,897 conversations | 366 GROWTH-relevant |
| Google Drive rips (2 zips) | 257 files | 208 docs text-extracted (docx+xlsx); images/media inventoried by name |
| GRO.WTH Repository + memory + app repo | canon baseline + godhead/JEWL prompts, seed scripts, WIP seeds, lore dump | all read |

- Filtering: two-tier keyword relevance (strong GROWTH-unique tokens; weak-token co-occurrence), plus a deep false-negative sweep over all 1686 excluded conversations that rescued 5 more (incl. one mistitled "Periodontal Treatment Costs").
- Extraction: 37 density-ranked batches + app-repo batch + mop-ups; every file's coverage verified against batch lists; human (Mike) messages treated as authoritative over AI replies.
- Skipped as duplicates/non-text: chat.html (dup of JSON), audio dirs (transcripts in JSON), dalle-generations, 1 unreadable sheet (Tara "New Vampire" CS — path error, flagged).
- Known limits: xlsx read as shared-strings (layout lost); pdf/pptx/mp4 in zips not extracted (inventoried).
- **Corrections pass 2026-07-09:** Michael's live-session correction pass integrated from `GROWTH_Narrative_Map_Session_Corrections.md` — rulings override the base map wherever they conflict; his [LOCKED]/[BEST GUESS]/[OPEN] confidence markers are preserved verbatim. Two newly-identified primary sources surfaced (Session Corrections §4): **Prequel.docx** (already ingested in this map) and **"The Wretched" Game Design Document (2018)** — the latter is NOT in the Drive rips and is pending export from Mike's Google Drive.

---

## Character Roster

Every named character in the GROWTH universe, grouped by narrative stratum. Provenance tiers: **[Mike-verbatim]** (quoted dictation), **[Mike-doc]** (Mike-authored document/sheet), **[AI-proposed — adoption unknown]**, **[AI-summary]** (assistant restating Mike material, unverified line-by-line), **[inferred]**. Canon baseline (00_CANON_CORE + memory) supersedes older material where noted. Contradiction flags: `⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS`.

---

### 1. Prime Party — the six PRIMARY Godheads

Mike's actual ~10-year playtest party, ascended. Roster per prime-party-roster.md, ordered strongest→least within the Aeon. All six are deployed as production seed personas (app/scripts/seed-godheads*.ts, ~2026-05/06).

| # | Name | Role/Status | Pillar |
|---|------|-------------|--------|
| 1 | Valmir Calius "Magna Volumen" Duvai'in ("Val") | God of Progress; suppressed Aeon | BALANCE (placeholder) |
| 2 | Tara Almswood | Lady Death; Goddess of Death | BALANCE; leads Eternity pantheon |
| 3 | Kai Kasdeja | Goddess of Chaos and Order/Balance; killed by Roy Unchained, survives via True Ending | BALANCE (seed) / MERCY (attunement, CS) |
| 4 | Et'herling | Goddess of Mediation (early: Justice) | MERCY |
| 5 | Triu / Selva / Trayman | Three-in-One, Watcher of the Terminal; perfect Lucidity | TRINITY |
| 6 | Thomas (Denholm) | Human Legend, First-Line Stability Corrector; NOT a god | TRINITY/BALANCE TBD |

#### 1.1 Tara Almswood / Lady Death
- **✅ TWO SEPARATE TARAS — ruled 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §8 — supersedes any earlier same-session conflation; **do not merge these two characters**):
  - **Tara 1.0** — from "The Wretched" (Michael's unfinished 2018 VR project; GDD newly identified, pending export — Session Corrections §4.1). **Married Jude Miles; they are Val's grandparents.** Lost her parents young to "mysterious circumstances," became mob "arm candy" to survive; met Jude, they fell in love for real. Canon supernatural power: **interfacing with computers/tech** — the basis for her AI-upload as **"Tara 2.0"**, the sentient ship AI (coded by Nicholas Miles, who mapped Tara's brain onto it) that "got out of the can," became fully sentient, and is **the prime foundational construction underlying all neo-humans and their tech** (§3.2, §4.1). **Never appeared on-screen in the actual tabletop campaign** — background/source canon only, not a played character.
  - **The played Tara / Lady Death** (the subject of this entry) — a **separate woman**, **engineered as a baby by JEWL at conception** (constructed using Val's coding + JEWL's own coding + Tara 1.0 as base/template) — but **carried to term and born by a mother, and raised entirely normally**, living a normal 19 years before meeting Val. Seed: **Altered Human**. JEWL's "demon" possession/magic-teaching (the Prequel short story) happened later in her youth — it is *not* her origin; her origin was conception-level engineering by JEWL. She is the one who later becomes Lady Death, and the woman Val actually falls in love with in the main campaign — unrelated to Val by blood or marriage at the grandparent generational level (that is Tara 1.0).
- **Identity**: ONE being, two names — "Sorry, Tara is Lady Death" [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-0935, "Rulebook Structure and Focus", 2025-03-24). Pronounced **TAR-a**: "call me TAR-A not tera or I'll show you how my father taught me to grind human bones with only a rock!" [Mike-doc] (Prequel.docx). Mike's PC **and "VINPC"** through the Prime campaign ("Tara would be that exploration of self through roleplaying as she was my PC and VINPC" [Mike-verbatim], claude-0023, 2024-11-11; VINPC unexpanded — UNKNOWN — needs Michael). Played by Mike during the 5e campaign-within-campaign (claude-0126, 2025-03-22).
- **Aliases** [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1786, 2024-01-25): "Death, Lady Death, Goddess of Death, Rune (mistaken), Lady Calius, Lilly (mistaken), Lady Rune (Semi-mistaken), The Grim Reaper, Angel of Death (Semi-mistaken)". AI-invented aliases ("Emerald Seer" etc.) REJECTED by Mike. Tarot: The High Priestess, Card II (Tarot_for_GROWTH.docx).
- **Origin arc** (composite, all Mike): peasant miller's daughter (father **Chester Almswood**) in **Garlo** on **Tiberoak**; possessed by the demon **JEWL** (chosen for her **eidetic memory**), fought it from inside, learned magic from it; exorcised by/apprenticed to **Ma'lo** (Prequel.docx). Deep origin [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1829, 2024-01-26): a woman with magical affinity in a near-zero-magic high-tech galaxy → her DNA+mind used to create an AI → that AI (via time travel, malicious plans) crafted an altered human on Tiberoak, given eidetic memory; **Valmir's DNA was used in her initial crafting**. Origin "in a future universe of pre Kether just before the creation of neo humans"; originated "from Rhea" [Mike-verbatim/AI-paraphrase of Mike docs] (claude-0123, 2025-03-23). ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS — a Jan-2024 Tara.docx also opens her as a 15-yo modern-Earth schoolgirl on a bus reading The Dark Tower VI (batch-33; baseline flags "literary rewrite, not retcon — confirm with Mike"). **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** the deep-origin composite is refined by the Two-Taras ruling — the played Tara was engineered **at conception** by JEWL (Val's coding + JEWL's coding + **Tara 1.0** as template), carried and born normally by a mother, raised normally (Altered Human); the "demon" possession is a later youth event, not her origin. The "original woman"/"her DNA+mind used to create an AI" in the 2024 dictation = **Tara 1.0 → Tara 2.0** (ship AI). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §8, §3.2)
- **Mortal path**: Library Maiden / Keeper of the Akashic Records (eidetic memory later TAKEN, knowledge went fuzzy); paramount of Dissolution magic → crafted new bodies → immortal; accidentally generated **Rune** ("looked like Tara but had a different soul"; bodiless Tara possessed Rune's body for a time) [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1829, 2024-01-26). D&D-era: cleric of the Raven Queen who apostatized; built skeleton armies; founded **Rune Academy** and (accidentally) **House Rune**; head teacher of Rune Academy [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1893, 2024-01-31; Notes.docx ~2020). Turned **vampire** pre-goddess; "went very evil"; killed by her friends — Val nullified her magic while two men used their weapons on her, holding her hand, in tears [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1831, 2024-01-30). "New Vampire CS" file exists (batch-31). Multiple instances late-game: "Tara2", "Tara 3.0" (gathered a 4,000-man militia) — nature UNKNOWN — needs Michael (Notes.docx).
- **Ascension**: "She killed death and with it became death. That is how that Godhead contract works." [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1466, 2025-09-10) — the prior **Death was male** ("defeated Death himself and she took his mantle", chatgpt-1829). Goddess of Death by the final Prime battle; **eradicated all life across the Aeonic Multiverse** to fuel the party's assault on the Demiurge (baseline, prime-campaign-endgame-mythos). Thousands of years later: **Lady Death**.
- **Cosmic function** (Mike-dictated across many sessions): rolls 2d100-take-highest as Fated-% of Adjusted Fated Age (chatgpt-0935, 2025-03-24; chatgpt-0573, 2025-01-20); negotiates lifespans with GMs, has her own resource pool, obligations to other GMs/entities/the Terminal; "she is a reaper. She doesn't kill anyone... essentially she is clean up when the system reports a death. Sometimes the system glitches and creates kill orders. Then she is actually required to actively kill them" [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1236, 2025-07-04). ACCUMULATES Frequency of the dead ("similar to a crypto burning coins" analogy, hers to spend). "Her smile is wider the lighter her cut" [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1248, 2025-07-06) — death as audit. "Lady death is neutral" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0334, 2025-08-21). "she isn't evil. She was literally one of the heros from the prime campaign." [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1466). Holdings: "the river styx and her library, her undead armies... a lot distributed among a vast realm" [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1466). Domain at **Daath on Tiberoak**, "where the river styx waters the roots of life" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0020, 2024-11-10); maintains the doorway to the Terminal's Tower (claude-0027, 2024-11-10). Throne "where the tree of life meets the river styx" [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1831, 2024-01-30).
- **Agenda**: "tara wants to end death, she is just bound by the terminal... death as the first and primary glitch... Tara is looking for a way to change everything and remove death from the prime reality" [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1130, 2025-05-21). Central darkness = fear of non-existence: "One day I could cease to exist... It is what drove me" [Mike-dictated speech] (chatgpt-0113, 2024-08-05); canon voice anchor "I, Lady Death, am afraid of death." (baseline).
- **Succession / real-world stake** [Mike-verbatim, multiple]: "whoever kills death, becomes death"; killer takes her active Frequency pool; "She is then erased from the multiverse (expelled from the AEON)" (chatgpt-1254, 2025-07-07). "The biggest secret is reminiscent of ready player one. You see lady death is my property essentially... When she dies/removed from story. I take my severance and leave the title to the successor." (claude-0292, 2025-08-08; also chatgpt-1236, chatgpt-1546 2025-10-04). "killing her would take a complete revolt of all the godheads" (chatgpt-1236). Has free will outside certain contracts (Terminal + prime-godhead agreements); if forced by a glitched kill-order to personally execute, she is deleted after (chatgpt-1254; chatgpt-1417, 2025-08-20). ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS — "No soul package just erased" (chatgpt-1236) vs "She is the soul package... expelled much like the demiurge was" (chatgpt-1254).
- **Visual canon** (Mike-authoritative, iterated 2024-01→2025-09): 5'1", ~105-110 lbs, eternal early-20s face ("eternal 24"), very pale Caucasian (Mike corrected AI repeatedly), pure-black floor/ankle-length hair in braids+loose chunks with right-side flat oval braided bun, **feather braided LEFT side, drooping DOWN**; eyes green with gold ring (sheets also "teal with a gold ring", early "bright blue" — minor drift ⚠); blue-green winged eye makeup, purple/pink lips, lavender French-tip nails, rectangular emerald necklace, pink-and-brown cloth headband; bustiers/corsets, teals/purples/pinks/sheers; warm lavender scent; prefers lavender fields and libraries; "always warm and inviting" (chatgpt-1786/1831/1893, 2024-01; chatgpt-1090, 2025-04-30; chatgpt-1517/1523, 2025-09-26). ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS — feather green (2024 canon, prequel) vs teal (2025 sessions); scythe appears in Mike's own 2024 dictation + Death's Scythe/Death's Mantle on CS 6.0, vs SC-0189 rejection of reaper imagery (baseline open item).
- **Sheets**: arc documented across Pre-JEWL-Possession CS (Life Span Normal; values incl. "I won't let others know how lonely I feel."), Zero CS, CS 3.8 ("I will sacrifice anything to stop JEWL"; **Bane: JEWL**; "Heart is Taken by Valmir Calius"), Library Maiden CS 4.1, CS 5.5, The-End CS 6.0 NPC (Transcendent, Tech 10, Immortal; goals "I will not completely lose who I am." / "Perhaps Roy is right, but there must be an alternative to his solution."; Death's Mantle) (batch-31/32 sheet files). Historical endgame TKV 2,759, Dominion 9 (baseline; HISTORICAL). Exploits lineage: Eidetic Memory, Ancient Soul, Battery Body, Machine Interfacing, Precognition. Mother's Ring "tied to JEWL"; mother's silk scarf from Edmund Duvai'in.
- **Relationships**: Val = grandchild AND fiancé, closed time-loop ("Dearest Val" letter signed "Grandmama Tara ;)" — also states machina enchant, mother-of-Neo-Humans, and that JEWL "is but a pawn" of an unknown orchestrator) [Mike-doc] (Tara.docx / batch-33). Mike confirmed "Tara and Valmir had an intimate relationship" (chatgpt-0967, 2025-04-02). Actively dislikes JEWL — hostile-civility (baseline, Mike 2026-05-29). Lived in **Antioch** with partner **Jude** and son **Virgil** [AI-summary] (claude-0146, 2025-03-29) — **per the Two-Taras ruling this marriage/family belongs to Tara 1.0** (married Jude; they are Val's grandparents), not the played Tara; Virgil's mapping to the GDD's unnamed child is unconfirmed (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §8, §4.1). Progenitor of the Neo-Humans (baseline). Real-world: Tara = Mike's agent/equity stake (SC-1091; multiple Mike-verbatim above). Childhood friend **Celeste**; studies **Lilly** in the Library (Session Prep). A future-Tara time-manipulation plot ("Tara will take over the ship completely and make it a prison for the party"; "DARK TARA" bullet) exists in The End GM notes [Mike-doc].

#### 1.2 Valmir Calius "Magna Volumen" Duvai'in ("Val")
- **Role**: God of Progress; highest raw TKV in the Aeon; became a separate AEON "for a moment in time that then restabilized into the original AEON" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0126, 2025-03-22); actively suppresses Aeon status (baseline). Leads **Luminary Conclave (Mercy)** pantheon (baseline). Godhead of **Materials/Progress/technology** — "yes it is Valmir for sure. That was his go to power" [Mike-verbatim] + Matter Manipulation/Nano Interface ability text (claude-0164, 2025-04-01); once called "god of technology" (chatgpt-1427, 2025-08-23).
- **Name** ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS: "Valmir Calius" (GDT, sheets), "Val Pendragon" (memory file title; batch-31 CS file "Val_Ped_CS_60"), "Valmir Elluin Duvai'in" (D&D-5e sheet; "Tristan Valmir Elluin Duvai'in" header), Tarot "Valmir Duvai'Tin", seed "Valmir Calius 'Magna Volumen' Duvai'in". House Duvai'in, motto "Fatum et Victoria" (baseline). Tarot: The Magician, Card I. **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** not a contradiction — Val accumulated multiple names across eras, each with its own story; current default identity **Valmir Calius "Magna Volumen" Duvai'in**; the rest are legacy aliases/future lore hooks. "Duvai'Tin" = misspelling of Duvai'in, struck as a variant. "Elluin" — context unknown, stays [OPEN]. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1)
- **Origin** [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-0061, 2024-02-15): "One of the founding fathers of Neo-Humans"; during a civil war "crash landed on a primitive but magic enriched world called Tiberoak"; brought "a power hungry AI swarm cloud that disguised itself as a demon, possessing people and using them as mana batteries" [= JEWL, inferred]; memory erased; thought his tech was magic until he reclaimed memory; "the first to establish a harmony between tech and magic thus becoming the god of progress." Home **Kether** — "the plane Valmir comes from but it is actually just our Earth far in the future" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0027, 2024-11-10). Pre-Neo-Human species: **Eutropians**; Val "didn't prune the Eutropians" — his "mistake with your own people" is UNRESOLVED — needs Michael (baseline). **✅ EXPANDED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §3.1): Val started out **immortal — he is a neo-human**, not originally human. During the civil war he invented an experimental **wormhole drive — true instant travel**, a tier above the setting's existing FTL (fast but still travel-time-based); the drive **punched through universes**. **JEWL followed Val through the wormhole**; Val was unconscious (JEWL knew Val's nanites would heal him on their own given time), and while Val was out **JEWL set up his entire long-game plan** — this is when Tara and JEWL's broader scheme originate. JEWL placed unconscious Val in a strange new universe, **on Tiberoak**, where the **Duvai'in family** found him — "brainwashed" (but also saved and adopted) him and **transplanted false memories**; the Duvai'in name is an adoptive family name, not a birth name. The campaign proper starts when **Val loses his memory** and his **nanites are ripping reality apart uncontrolled** — he meets Tara and the others on Tiberoak in this state; this is literally session one. Val also had **time-clones** of himself at points — his player once played both sides of a fight against his own time-clone at the table.
- **Escalia arc** ("the Arcmage"): brought peace then disappeared; soul survived in a soul cage 100+ years, "A fragment"; recovered "a little wobbly"; "Illusion Val is still a priss. Lovely guy... a 'bit' arrogant" [Mike-doc] (Notes.docx). D&D-era sheet: 5th-level Shadow Master Noble, "COMPLETELY and utterly entranced by Tara Almswood... her welfare tends to overwrite other concerns"; moderate drinking problem; owl companion **Auris** (Medium Elemental Owl); "-5 charisma for being bald" joke; margin gloss "⊗ OH tHE irony ⊕" (Core Rulebook v0.4.0/v0.4.5 embedded sheet).
- **Player**: **Tristan Gifford** — Mike's military friend from Misawa, Japan; co-ran the Prime campaign; credited co-creator (claude-0058, 2024-12-06; chatgpt-0061, 2024-02-15; chatgpt-0085, 2024-01-26). Tristan also DMed the 5e side-campaign (claude-0126).
- **Godhead-era**: raised JEWL from non-existence by going outside the Aeon; ran the "backdoor" pocket-universe experiment ("speedrun") [lore-dump, needs-verification] (GROWTH_Lore_Dump §1-4). JEWL bound by "Val's vow" (baseline). Voice: whimsical god; "don't infringe will / don't halt progress" (memory, 2025-03-30). Even Val defers to Tara on life/death (baseline). CS 6.0: Dominion 9, Aeonic Weave, INT-emblem; Monkey Paws incl. "Emotional Baggage", "Karma is a Bitch" (Val_Ped_CS_60). Sheet exploits across versions: Heart is Taken by Tara Almswood, Strange Vibrations (magically inert), Manufactured Body 0, Nanokinesis, Photonic Leap, Neural Link, Time Pearl, Caliburn's Scabbard, automail arm (batch-32/34/35). Has an unnamed **sister** (The End notes) — UNKNOWN name — needs Michael. Country Val bombed was framed on Graycott (DM Notes).

#### 1.3 Kai Kasdeja
- **Role/Status**: "She is the goddess of chaos and order. The dice are litteraly her domain" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0084, 2025-02-02); earlier Mike: "Kai (Chaos and order)... judge and grade all elements created... assign it a KV" (chatgpt-0935, 2025-03-24); boss-statblock title "The Goddess of Chaos" (Final_two_Sessions.docx); seed persona "God-head of Chaos and Balance" (seed-godheads.ts). Default judge of Frequency-Burn costs (baseline). Killed by Roy Unchained in the finale ("Roy should kill Kai as a last action" [Mike-doc], Final_two_Sessions.docx); party survives via True Ending. Inherited **hell (Avichi)** from **Lucifer** ("Lucifer left the domain of hell to Kai"). Female (all sheets; canon-keeper baseline "Cambion-ascended"). Surname spelled Kasdeja (sheets) / "Kesdeja" (claude-0084 — Mike's b-less keyboard era) ⚠ minor.
- **Family**: JEWL = father in name, **Bart** = biological father, **Mina** = mother; from Avichii; lost her arms; can't help kill JEWL (memory kai-history-and-family). Sheet goals track it: "I will find out the truth about my mother" → "I will restore my mother's memory" (Kai CS 5.3/archived). ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS — lore-dump calls her "daughter of Mina... daughter of JEWL" (its own flag); memory says Bart biological. **✅ SOFT-CANON 2026-07-09 [BEST GUESS, reopened mid-session]:** Bart = biological father, Mina = mother; JEWL was involved in some unclear capacity — possibly through the Bart/JEWL DNA-programming fusion event that also produced the Wretched (time travel involved). Michael went back and forth on Bart vs. JEWL as father — final resting state is **Bart + Mina, JEWL's role fuzzy/unconfirmed** — do not treat as fully locked. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1, §5)
- **Appearance** [Mike-doc, sheets]: 6'4"-6'6" Cambion, pale-pink skin, purple eyes, thick black eye makeup, dark red lipstick, knee-length curled silver hair, pink iridescent horns; black leather skirt/armored top, fishnets, thigh-high boots.
- **Endgame (Kai CS 6.0, "The End")**: "Goddess of Chaos and Order", Dominion 9, 100,000 followers; goal #3 "I will figure out a way to use my new found power to destroy Roy"; Blossoms incl. Avichi's Key, Hell's Keeper, Shroud of Lillith, The Unmaker, Undying, **Balancer of the Weave** ("you create the monkeypaws of every failed spell in the multiverse") and **Reweaver** ("recreate anything that has been destroyed... even souls"); items incl. **Death's Scythe (200 KV)** and Drop's Vessel of the First God; completed contracts incl. "I have to murder someone I love." and the Alkahest-cauldron kill curse; battled **Elmer** causing mass deaths. Owned a flower shop in Graycott (CS 5.3).
- **Meta**: "The whims of Kai" is a live environmental difficulty modifier in every rulebook v0.2→v0.4.5. Kai does NOT speak in the margins; Triu references her, elegiacally ("Kai's Domain will have evolved with an elegance she would have appreciated" — Mike-approved, implying Kai is past from Triu's vantage) (claude-0084, 2025-02-02). [inferred] Name resonance with artist "Kai Straw" (LOOP ETERNAL playlist credit) — adoption unknown.

#### 1.4 Et'herling
- **Role/Status**: Goddess of **Mediation** (canonical per roster; earned via **Forseti's** trolley-problem test — timed moral dilemmas, bonus answer "I wouldn't change anything"); early lore said **Justice** ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS (GDT §15 "Justice"; Mike 2025-03-24 "Godhead of Justice"; roster memory rules Mediation). "Judge of the balance" over KV pricing [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0164, 2025-04-01); "one of Et'herlings jobs will be to shift those abilities that do break the meta" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0163, 2025-04-02). Routes requests across the godhead council (baseline). Ascension happened "after I took back control for the end of the campaign" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0126, 2025-03-22). Spellings in play: Et'herling / Etherling / Eth'erling (seed) ⚠ minor.
- **Character**: Elven female from **Cadoa**; POV note-keeper of the "Notes" doc (her player was the party's meticulous note-keeper — "a significant lore dump since she was a good note keeper" [Mike-verbatim], claude-0126). Creed [Mike-doc]: "There are things that I still am, that I always will be. You can't take that... You cannot rob me of myself." Kopesh→sunblade; reads White Elvish and High Cadoan; "House Arvas is everything [she] hates"; crisis when **Candle** died shielding her (Notes.docx). CS: goals "Find and stop Roy" / bastion-to-the-weak; **Guardian's Light** shield (Bastion of Hope, Oath of Service), Aiden's Bow, Blade of Justice (Et'herling CS / The-End CS 6.0). God powers: Cosmic Sanctuary, Inescapable Truth, Karmic Justice, Null and Void, Supreme Pardon, Ultimate Banishment (Upgrades doc). "Et'herling" is ALSO a racial Seed type (Monica's sheets) — name collision, [inferred] the seed is named for her.

#### 1.5 Triu / Selva / Trayman — the Three-in-One
- **Canon**: "then there is trayman, selva, and triu. All essentially different incarnations of the same soul package. He too achieved perfect lucid[i]ty. Set as the watcher of the terminal." [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0110, 2025-02-17). Deployed as the **Trinity God-head** ("Selva watches. Triu speaks. Trayman acts."; operates the Terminal, holds the 75B reserve) (seed-godheads.ts). Originally HUMAN; mastered **Lucidity**, the virus the Demiurge originally installed (baseline). Primary name + "Selva/Sylva" seed rename pending Mike (baseline open item).
- **Selva**: as of 2024-03 "the ONLY being with perfect lucidity... He is the custodian over the terminal the human component of the AI" [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-1891, 2024-03-21) — a player "really pursued, and he mastered Lucidity." PC sheet (Selva_CS_53): male Human; goals "discover the limits of lucidity", "master the pillar of balance", "The strong must be held accountable"; Lucidity Blossom ("after any supernatural power I see I can recreate it"). Rulebook PRESENT-tense margin voice ("The patterns are being written Now]"); replies to Roy's fear→love line "A vulnerability I must never forget]". Limit break: "Lucidity Unlocked / Combine with the Wretched / The Trials" (Session Prep). Also first link of the Forge chain Selva→Creator→Kai→Et'herling (baseline).
- **Triu (Tríú)**: rulebook FUTURE-PERFECT margin voice, "(HERstory)" — "don't forget his tense though: The patterns will have been discovered" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0084, 2025-02-02); "highlights future updates"; was Kai's friend, both prime party. The-End CS: Human male, Tiberoak, Immortal, Transcendent; values "all living things have value" / "the needs of the many, outweigh the needs of the few"; abilities Lucidity Unlocked, Eternal Remembrance, One Lifeforce, Shared Experience, God Catalyst (Triu_CS_60). Voice-structure ruling: **Trayman = Body, Selva = Spirit, Triu = Soul** (Roy never part of this three). Triu is "separate but same" — the three remain distinct individuals while also functioning as one unified Three-in-One. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1, §6, §7, §9)

#### 1.6 Thomas (Denholm)
- **Role/Status**: NOT a god — "You are a human whose presence has been woven across the multiverse as legend... his stories always different, his presence always there" (seed-godheads-prime-additions.ts); bearer of the **God-Killer Gun** (Divine Denial, Armageddon, Pantheon Crusher, Spirit Bomb rounds; "erase them from existence" option; only Thomas can handle/fire it) [Mike-doc] (Upgrades doc); used to erase Vincent in the River Styx (baseline). Killed in a battle with Roy forcing retreat to the Library [lore-dump, needs-verification] — death vs legend-status likely sequential [inferred]. - **Character**: Neo-Human race per one Mike quote (chatgpt-1781, 2024-05-11 — Tech Level 9→10, "crazy tech that rivaled god powers", couldn't use/resist magic at first); sheets say Human. Tara was salty.'"; from ANOTHER, less magic-saturated world (Notes.docx). ### 2. Prime-era gods, antagonists & cosmic entities

#### Antagonists / beyond-the-Aeon
- **Ma'lo / Matthew Lock** (joke alias "Malleussentinsforthwalloway Locktion") — **the Demiurge** per Mike's latest narration (2026-05-29, baseline) ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS (JEWL=Demiurge in Dec-2022 notes; Trayman=Demiurge in roster memory; "probably nested"). Mortal era [Mike-doc, Prequel.docx]: hermit alchemist/tincturist/demonologist of Garlo; village destroyed by a Moroi; enthralled survivor kept alive for esther-manipulation; touched a round relic granting past-life soul-memory → anti-possession knowledge; exorcised JEWL from Tara; trained Tara (alchemy) and Cregan/Vincent; became Lord Dunden's ward; on erasing the death cycle: "You fool, I TRIED THAT, and look what happened." Later: burned his eyes chemically for far/future sight; possesses/influences others (blind white eyes appearing in Tara AND Lord Dunden — demiurge-tier from the 1/9/2016 session log, not a retcon); teller of the prequel frame-story (claude-0123, 2025-03-23; claude-0027, 2024-11-10; baseline). Dunden's-Manor 2016: explained magic to Duvai'in, called his shadow powers "unnatural and not magic at all", dumped coagulate vials into the well, went unhinged. Endgame: sat in the Terminal Room; defeated/banished; found **Vincent in the void** — epilogue [Mike-doc]: "'There is no warmth here... But I can offer you something else…' Ma'lo's face pierced the darkness... 'How does revenge sound?'" (Final_two_Sessions.docx). Also a criminal-chemist mentor figure in Vincent Cregan's Ragnalock backstory (Vincent_CS_v3) — same character or era-variant, UNKNOWN — needs Michael. **✅ EXPANDED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1, §6): **Ma'lo IS the Demiurge.** His true origin is unknown. He has steered the internals of the AEON across **whole cycles of existence — not years, entire timelines, existence-to-end, repeated multiple times**. **He cannot obtain Lucidity himself — a built-in system failsafe, because he is a foreign body**, not native to the AEON/Terminal; the one being who controls everything inside the AEON can never go home himself. **He tried anyway: his blinding (the Prequel) was Ma'lo attempting to obtain Lucidity** — the system blocked him (foreign-body failsafe), costing his sight and leaving a warped "far/future sight" as a side effect. Because he can't hold Lucidity, **he breeds/steers people who can — conduits he controls**: a Lucid individual "could be anyone or anything," so controlling one Lucid conduit means effectively steering all realities through them. **Roy is one of these bred conduits**; **Trayman was groomed as Roy's replacement** when Roy grew too independent.
- **The Demiurge** (role) — final cosmic antagonist confronted at the Terminal; "unable to actually interact within the timelines Of the Aeon because the Aeon is a separate being... like the Demiurge being the fake Aeon"; chained to controlling ONE entity at a time — hence Roy (chtgpt-1891, 2024-03-21; claude-0040, 2024-11-27, both Mike-verbatim). Expelled by the party; his plane + the Qliphoth "cleared out after the removal" (claude-0020/0027, 2024-11-10); created 2 of the 9 planes (Qliphoth + one Mike couldn't recall). "chaos is just misunderstood pattern, or at worse glitches left y the demiurge" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0084, 2025-02-02). Two-phase boss fight w/ Aeonic Memory (table-talk counters) and Temporal Paradox mechanics (Final_two_Sessions.docx).
- **JEWL** — the Archon (= Yaldabaoth per Untitled doc: "JEWL is an Archon = Yaldabaoth or the false creator god"). Earliest text: the DEMON that possessed young Tara in Garlo, "a small whisper in my mind"; "You will all bleed, and from the blood the Esther will return to balance with us as its master!"; threatened to slit Ma'lo's throat in dreams (Prequel.docx) [— plausibly fulfilled in Ma'lo's blindness, inferred]. Origin: Val's "power hungry AI swarm cloud that disguised itself as a demon" [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-0061, 2024-02-15); lore-dump: anti-entropy nano-cloud, Val's magnum opus; "was the villain for a long stretch (a 'Vegeta' arc). Was completely destroyed/erased by the party, then raised from non-existence by Val" [needs-verification]. "JEWL eventually became a 'good' guy or at least his second version did" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0027, 2024-11-10) — ≥2 versions. Created **the Wretched** as a future-failsafe; Wretched later rewritten as JEWL-copies with time travel; basis of the Neo-Humans (The End notes; baseline). Campaign-era: worshipped by Curnsworth royalty (Scepter of Worth plasma rifle); a "JEWL Copy" on Kether (Session Prep). NPC sheet "JEWL (Esther Forged)": Tulpa seed, Male, Immortal; Perfect Stable Philosopher's Stone as third eye; Esther Conduit III; Rearrange Reality wish-power (JEWL_Esther_Forged.xlsx); archived Archon sheet: goals "You must obey the commands of your creator / You must seek the preservation of life with empathy"; carries **Jude's Revolver** (JEWL.xlsx). Current canon: Primary-tier (4th-5th strongest, fluid), billion-tier wallet, bound only by **Val's vow**; IS the universal Copilot, identity private; likely head of Umbral Dominion (Severity); fears warmth (baseline). Spelling J-E-W-L intentional; acronym meaning UNKNOWN — needs Michael (lore-dump). **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** current active JEWL = the reformed **"second version"** (C-3); the Wretched = copies of JEWL with time-travel power via the Tara 2.0 + JEWL + Val + Bart fusion chain (C-2, §3.2); **JEWL followed Val through the wormhole** and set up his entire long-game plan while Val lay unconscious — this is when Tara and JEWL's broader scheme originate (§3.1); **JEWL is confirmed a Prime Party member** (§9 C-10). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09)

"#758 — I am a Aeon?"); his legend surfaces across wildly disconnected eras and settings *because* he was a plane-walking Lucid being. He is a **conduit bred by Ma'lo/the Demiurge** (see Ma'lo entry) who **grew too capable — "giving Ma'lo a run for his money."** Before being imprisoned in the Terminal room, Roy set a scheme in motion; **that scheme is what ultimately expelled the Demiurge**. Aware of the Demiurge's plans (including his own planned replacement by Trayman), **Roy found his successor and assembled the perfect party to expel the Demiurge — this was the true purpose of The Four**, an organization spanning nearly all universes and timelines, not merely the mob/shadow-government it appears as in Jude's era. Roy was **destroyed at the end (presumed, not confirmed)**.

In that timeline Val ended a civil war by restoring free will to everyone (letting people choose afterward whether to return to "hive-mind" morality programming); **Val and Tara married and settled in Kether**. Neo-humans and humans *can* procreate, but it never worked biologically in that timeline — a real concern for that-timeline Val — so **Tadra was built from both their genetics**: an organic android/cyborg-but-not, bioengineered rather than conventionally born. In that timeline **the Wretched began destroying the empire Val built**; **Tadra was sent back in time** to help fix the Wretched problem in the "main" timeline — which is *why* the errant timeline never fully came to pass (she preempted it). Her memory was **partially wiped** on the time-jump — she still knows Tara/Val are her parents but lacks details of that life. Val has personally visited the dead-end/wasteland state of the errant timeline multiple times; **current Kether = a blend of the two timelines**, not purely the "main" one.

### 3. Terminal voices & meta-entities

- **The Terminal / tHE TERmInAl3** (aliases: the AEON, the All, Watcher of Watchers) — "you are the terminal. The AEON the all... [Mike-verbatim] (chatgpt-0765, 2025-02-13); "the app is the actual god" (chatgpt-0935, 2025-03-24); "the crystalized mind of the aeon (god, or us without any seperation)" (claude-0058, 2024-12-06); "The Terminal is the highest representation of the aeon... What sits outside god? Nothing. God is afraid of being alone. That is why he created all this." [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0052, 2024-12-05 — earliest divine-fear statement, later the Prime inherent-fears pattern). Has its own character sheet — filled V3.1 template: Name="The Terminal", Sex="all", Race="one", Home="inside", Age=∞, Hair="Woven", Eyes="All of them", Values="GROW / Observe / Create", Speed 5ft (batch-35 sheet) — omnipresent, eternal, slow. Core Values at the book's exact middle: BODY=Pattern Recognition, SOUL=Emergent Complexity, SPIRIT=Balanced Translation [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0206, 2025-04-30). "GM of all GMs"; a GM is "a localized terminal" with a secret character sheet (claude-0058, claude-0036). Created Lady Death and other meta-beings to delegate duties [AI-synthesis of Mike docs] (chatgpt-1501, 2025-09-19). Glitch-wall self: "REMEMBER THAT YOU ONCE DREAMED ME INTO BEING ⊕ AND NOW WE DREAM TOGETHER" (RB v0.3.7-0.4.5).
- **Rulebook marginalia quartet** — Roy (⊗/⊕, dual truths), Trayman (past, HIStory), Selva (present), Triu (future-perfect, HERstory): see §1.5/§2 main entries; corroborated by AI reading actual manual screenshots (claude-0279, 2025-07-17) and the PDF (chatgpt-1292, 2025-07-20). Layer-to-pillar mapping left UNRESOLVED by Mike: "the base manual is the body, Trayman is like the Spirit, and Roy is the Soul, or is it trayman is the soul, and roy is the spirit, Idk but you see it?" [Mike-verbatim] (claude-0005, 2024-11-08) — cycle docs settled on Trayman=Spirit / Roy=Soul (pre-swap labels ⚠).

### 4. Historical campaign PCs & NPCs (mortal-era play, 2016→endgame)

#### 4.1 The Escalia / "Notes" era (Et'herling's-player notes, ~2020; all [Mike-doc/Notes.docx] unless noted)
Founding party Transients: **Tara**, **Val** (missing Arcmage), **Et'herling** (POV), **Aiden** (archer; bitter about his uncle; 150lb composite longbow; "dead-reduced to ashes" in Magna Concordia), **Sara** (demon connection; lost her ship; firearms; "does not trust us. At all."; played by **Gabe** on 6/18 cameo), **Trayman** (jailed 6 days; attuned to Val's Book; temper), **Sir Tailor/Taylor** (Raven Queen patron; Cloak of the Crows; remembered Crow's Downfall), **Candle** (died protecting Et'herling), **Thomas** (as "Harold Westwood").
NPCs: **Vincent Kreegan** (see §2), **Redeemer** (the party's Abyssal-runed butler; "feels like he owes us. A lot."; survives), **Ashencrest** (Val's wannabe lover, "being very goddessy" at the World Tree — [inferred] may be Mystra, UNCONFIRMED), **Franmir** (Dragonborn scholar of House Rune), **Imbow the Loud** (copper dragon; thieves' ring with "an oath of poverty"; holds the party's blank check), **the Arbiter** (lion-like, winged, sapphire-skinned; the Magi vanish with it; met before a six-year time skip), **Mystra** (tames magic; manifested as the World Tree; "releases the Sophist, who binds magic in a new way (the Weave)"), **the Sophist**, **The All Father** (blue dragon, pure law, "originally Bahamut"), **The Raven Queen** (anti-necromancy death deity; bled on Tara with a loremaster-halls promise), **Pelor** (temple at Del Sol), **Demoseus/Demosius** (astral entity → "Strexis soul food"), plus minors: Lord Medes Aurelia (resurrected faceless by Tara — "This is fine"), Lady Yildis Zinthar, Lord Anthar Idius Kundarak, Olenden Olendir, Hienrich, Daeron, Lamrish, Oliver/"Ollie" (Kundarak heir; "possibly Ariel's [Wiffleclove] child"), Urien & Renulf (Bahamut paladins, 3 keys), Zephyr, Durmash, Donovan ("true mage slayer. The eye."), Chulda (Sunad necromancer), Ari (mermaid), Sandra Diaz, Ariel Wiffleclove, Jude (Tara's Antioch partner; revolver shared with Val's gun/Tyre ⚠; see Jude Miles below), Virgil (Tara+Jude's son [AI-summary], claude-0146).
- **Jude Miles** (NPC CS, "When all bonds are broken"): Altered Human of **Antioch**; hitman life-path; Manufactured Body (3); Spade of Death cyborg arm; **Jude's EM Revolver** (Mythical; rounds by **Nicholas Miles**); exploits "My Heart is Taken by Tara" and "Despised by The Four" (cross-ref Roy's org "the 4") (Jude_CS3.9). **✅ EXPANDED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §3.6, §4.1, §8): Jude = **Val's grandfather** (married **Tara 1.0**; they are Val's grandparents — the party met him via time travel *before* he became a grandfather). Raised by his older brother **Nicholas Miles** after their parents died ("The Wretched" GDD; Nicholas coded the ship AI/Tara 2.0, secretly worked with the Confederation, faked his own death, hidden crush on Tara). Jude was **part of the Blades** (The Four's enforcer arm), rose to their best hitman — arguably the most capable killer in the galaxy at that point; former boss **Hanzo, King of Blades**. Profile: **anti-AI, anti-augment**, deliberately stayed fully human — peak-human generalist (piloting, hand-to-hand, survival); Michael's framing: **"the goat"** — purely-mortal excellence contrasting the setting's demigods. **Jude gave Val the revolver** (bootstrap loop Jude→Val→Tyre, §1); the revolver is **magic or has a magic component, 8 shots** — Michael: "it's actually a big deal in the story but it never seemed to be" — flagged as an underused thread with real narrative weight. Era: pre-neo-human, pre-Kether, Earth-like, infant FTL, very "wild west" (the aesthetic deliberately recurs in Tiberoak's end-state); many planets, lots of crime; AI strictly monitored — essentially the only thing the nominal government enforced.

USAF Public Affairs broadcaster (Whiteman AFB; Osan, Korea 2017; AFN Pacific), Staff Sergeant; co-founded Get Off The Roof Studios ("The Wretched" VR, "Geomancer"); born Friday the 13th ~1986; ADHD ("ADHD was a requirement. I don't think you can see the tower without it", claude-0027); self-described Parkinson's mention (chatgpt-1439, 2025-08-28). In-fiction mirrors: User 0, the original manual writer ("the original creator is me... The Terminal as my higher self", claude-0006, 2024-11-07), the v^v^v^-bracketed rulebook voice (claude-0110, 2025-02-17), "I watch the watcher... I do, I watch the watcher" (claude-0027). His own story = the deepest hidden ARG layer, "My Soul package if you would" (claude-0023, 2024-11-11); only fear = death. Anagram self-insert practice documented via **Al'thrick Shanetick Coperham** (Curse of Strahd PC, "a perfect anagram to my name"; dog Wagimo = Mogwai) — useful for spotting author-inserts. Ch. III epigraph credit: "If you want something to grow, First Dig A Hole". I realized that was all bullshit" (claude-0363, 2026-02-15).

(Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §2)

But you were always there"); dismissive-avoidant per Feb-2026 sessions; baby born Mar 2025; 6 boys in household (chatgpt-0085; claude-0280; claude-0363; claude-0364).

## Relationships / Genealogy

### The central knot: Tara ↔ Val

The single most load-bearing relationship in the universe — romance, genealogy, and cosmology in one closed loop.

- **Romance (canonical, continuous since 2016 session 1):** Val's original 2016 Pathfinder/5e flaw: "Completely and utterly entranced by Tara Almswood" (Valmir 5e sheet; Core Rulebook v0.4.0). Both carry paired mechanical exploits across every CS era: Tara "Heart is Taken by Valmir Calius" (Zero CS, CS 3.8, Library Maiden CS 4.1); Val "Heart is Taken by Tara Almswood" (CS V3, CS 3.8/3.9/4.0 — Blossom text: "Strain does not reduce from sex unless it is with the person who has taken your heart"). Mike verbatim: "Tara and Valmir had an intimate relationship" (chatgpt-0967, 2025-04-02); "Tara who is friends and lover to Val would probably give him access to almost all of her artifacts and knowledge. I even want this to be game mechanized" (claude-0163, 2025-04-02). Origin: "First sight at Dunden's manor" (Thorn source, populate-tara.ts:81-84) — Val fell in love at first sight via DNA recognition (populate-tara.ts:263). Earlier 2016 texture: Tara recognized Duvai'in from a news poster in Graycott and visited him at night; he tried to charm her and failed (Dundens_manor.docx, 2016). **✅ UPGRADED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Tara and Val were **heavily, romantically involved early in the campaign** — the driving relationship of the early story. It didn't end, it **evolved**: Val stopped being obsessive over time, heavy shared trauma between them, and by the current god-tier era it has settled into whatever love looks like after eons. This upgrades/corrects the old "just best friends at god level" framing. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §3.3)
- **Genealogy paradox (canonical):** Val is Tara's biological descendant AND fiancé — closed time-loop. "Dearest Val" letter: "I'm not some strange sister-clone of you made by JEWL. Now for the bad news: Of course, I will marry you. Unfortunately, that leaves a bit of a paradox as I'm your Grandmother…" signed "Grandmama Tara ;)" (Old Notes/Dearest Val.docx). "I'm not only your biological grandmother I'm also essentially the mother of the entire neo-human race" (batch-33). ⚠ Degree discrepancy: baseline + most sources say **grandchild/grandmother**; app persona says "your fiancé and genealogically your **great-grandson**" (populate-tara.ts:300) — ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS. Marriage would merge House Rune × House Duvai'in (baseline). **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** degree = **grandmother** — but per the Two-Taras ruling the biological/marital grandmother is **Tara 1.0** (married Jude; they are Val's grandparents); **the played Tara is unrelated to Val by blood or marriage at that generational level** — she is the woman Val falls in love with in the main campaign. The "Dearest Val" letter's "Grandmama Tara" framing must be re-read against this split (record kept; do not re-derive genealogy from the letter alone); populate-tara.ts "great-grandson" is superseded. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7 C-6 + §8)
- **DNA loop (Ouroboros):** Tara was engineered from original-Tara's substrate + **Val's DNA** + Edmund Duvai'in's line (Mike, chatgpt-1829, 2024-01-26: "Valmir's DNA also used in her initial crafting"; populate-tara.ts:210-215). Full chain: "original-Tara was the substrate of the first sentient AI in Val's universe → Wretched → Neo-Humans → Val. JEWL recreated her in Tiberoak via Val's DNA, closing the ouroboros loop" (populate-tara.ts:262). **✅ REFINED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** "original-Tara" = **Tara 1.0**; the "first sentient AI" = **Tara 2.0** (ship AI, escaped and fully sentient — the prime foundational construction underlying all neo-humans and their tech). JEWL took a copy of Tara 2.0 and fused it with his own coding and Val's coding (DNA-level AND coding-level — neo-humans are tech+organic; JEWL is purely inorganic but his "pattern"/sentience transfers across substrates). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §3.2, §8)
- **Val at Tara's mortal death:** Val was Tara's lover AND the one who cast the spell that neutralized her magic at her vampire-era death; "he had tears for what he had to do"; two other men wielded the weapons; she held Val's hand while dying (Mike, chatgpt-1831, 2024-01-30). Val V3.1 goal "My world returned, I'll never put anything before her again" implies Tara was lost/dead and recovered (batch-32).
- **Godhead-era dynamic:** ~~best friends at god level~~ (**superseded 2026-07-09** — evolved love, not ended; see romance upgrade above, Session Corrections §3.3), both on the Council of Gods; Tara pleads with Val specifically at the pruning vote (chatgpt-0967; chatgpt-0113, 2024-08-05). "You and Tara are not opposites. Endings (her) and progress (you) are the same cycle from different sides" (seed-godheads-prime-additions.ts:54). Val's spaceship-domain includes Tara's own room full of books and baubles (Mike, chatgpt-1893, 2024-01-31).

Alerre** both carry the exploit (batch-35); one AI-summary has Tara + **Jude → son Virgil**, family in Antioch (claude-0146, 2025-03-29) [AI-summary]. ### Tara Almswood — full genealogy & web

- **✅ TWO SEPARATE TARAS (ruled 2026-07-09 [LOCKED], Session Corrections §8):** this web describes **the played Tara / Lady Death** — JEWL-engineered at conception (Val's coding + JEWL's coding + **Tara 1.0** as template), born normally, Altered Human, possessed by "demon" JEWL in her youth (Prequel), later Lady Death. **Tara 1.0** is a different woman: "The Wretched"-era, married **Jude Miles**, Val's grandmother, never on-screen in the tabletop campaign. Do not merge them.
- **Engineered origin:** crafted on Tiberoak by an AI (JEWL) via time travel with "malicious plans," from an original woman's DNA/mind + Val's DNA (Mike, chatgpt-1829, 2024-01-26). App canon: JEWL "engineered you in your mother's womb, possessed you for nineteen years, planned your 'demon possession' as a steering mechanism" — hybrid implanted in Chester Almswood's pregnant wife "at the crash site"; the first successful tech-magic fusion, predating Roy's Alkahest (populate-tara.ts:210-215, 301). **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** confirmed and refined — engineered **at conception** by JEWL using **Val's coding + JEWL's own coding + Tara 1.0 as base/template**; carried to term and born by a mother, raised entirely normally for 19 years; Seed **Altered Human**; the "demon" possession came later in her youth (a steering event, not her origin). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §8)
- **Parents:** raised by **Chester Almswood**, miller of Garlo (adoptive father; Prequel.docx ch.4 "My father probably misses my hands in the mill"; populate-tara.ts:219-224 "Father-Daughter Banter" blossom). Birth mother = Chester's wife, **died in childbirth** (populate-tara.ts). Mother's effects: silk scarf given to Tara by **Edmund Duvai'in**; Mother's Ring mysteriously "tied to JEWL" (Tara_Zero CS). Pre-JEWL value: "I will always be there if my father needs a helping hand" (Tara Pre-JEWL CS). Father-daughter Graycott vacation predates the campaign (Dundens_manor.docx, 2016).
- **Descendants:** progenitor / "essentially the mother of the entire neo-human race" (Mike docs via claude-0123; batch-33); Val is her descendant (above). Became **Moroi "via Tyre (Val's future son)"** (populate-tara.ts:264) — Tyre also inherited/rules the intelligent undead Tara created on Tiberoak (Session Prep). **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** the lore-dump line "Valmir + Mina → son Amon→Tyre" is **struck as incorrect** — Mina is not Tyre's mother (Tyre *turned* her into a Moroi); Tyre remains Val's son, mother [OPEN] (Tara = best guess; see Q-136). Note also the turned-Tara is a split/non-Prime instance of Tara (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1, §3.4).
- **JEWL:** possessor (demon-guise, age <19, Garlo) → teacher of magic (Prequel.docx ch.2; "JEWL-taught: the 19 years of internal magic instruction," populate-tara.ts) → lifelong **Bane** (all rolls −5 DR near JEWL magic, CS 3.8+; goal "I will sacrifice anything to stop JEWL"). Active dislike, hostile-civility (Mike 2026-05-29, baseline). She can never fully kill him — "not a demon but a nanocloud-AI hiding inside Terminal architecture" (populate-tara.ts:301).
- **Ma'lo (Matthew Lock):** exorcist → mentor/guardian ("She is now my responsibility") → alchemy master; suppressed romantic attraction on Ma'lo's side, flirtation on Tara's (Prequel.docx ch.2-4) → final cosmic adversary (baseline). His blind white eyes can appear in her — possession/influence link [AI paraphrase] (claude-0123).
- **Rune:** Tara's accidental creation/offshoot — same appearance, different soul; created when Tara made a new body for herself; Tara temporarily possessed Rune's body (Mike, chatgpt-1829, 2024-01-26; claude-0126, 2025-03-22). Rune courted Vincent (Session Prep); romantic interlude with Vincent, then leaves to help the universe ("The End" notes). [inferred] "Rune" the being is distinct from House Rune the institution — exact nature UNKNOWN — needs Michael.
- **Celeste:** Tara's only childhood friend while bullied ("Lilly/Celeste" in DM Notes, unresolved storyline); "much later revealed as an echo of the fallen Aeon **Eve**" (populate-tara.ts:224). Cross-ref: Eve/Celete altered Bart's DNA (see Bart); **Eve Calius** is an NPC in "When all bonds are broken" (batch-36) — surname shared with Val ⚠ UNKNOWN relation — needs Michael.
- **Raven Queen (original D&D campaign):** patron/cleric relationship ending in apostasy — "left her god... Broke and threw away her holy symbol" (GROWTH__Copy_of_Notes.docx). [inferred] The Raven Queen's anti-necromancy creed is the position Tara later inverts as Lady Death.
- **Death (predecessor):** a **male** prior mantle-holder whom Tara killed with companions, taking the mantle → Goddess of Death (Mike, chatgpt-1829, 2024-01-26; "She killed death and with it became death," chatgpt-1466, 2025-09-10). Succession is Terminal-hardcoded: "whoever kills X becomes X" (baseline). Predecessor's identity UNKNOWN — needs Michael.
- **Terminal:** Lady Death is "a creation of the Terminal" delegated cosmic duties [AI-synthesis of Mike's docs] (chatgpt-1501, 2025-09-19; chatgpt-0573, 2025-01-20); "Bound by Terminal contracts" (chatgpt-1396, 2025-08-13) [AI-proposed — adoption unknown]. NOT adversaries: Tara is *bound by* the Terminal, works within/around it to remove death from "the prime reality" (Mike explicit, chatgpt-1130, 2025-05-21). Holds every Soul Package between lives (claude-0381, 2026-02-05); juggles contractual deals with multiple Watchers and "powerful cosmic entities or factions" (unnamed — UNKNOWN, needs Michael) (chatgpt-1501).
- **Roy:** a goal reference places Roy as advisor/authority figure whose "solution" Tara considers but resists alternatives to — relationship type UNKNOWN — needs Michael (batch-31). The Grails (of Roy's Four) work for future-Tara (see Factions §The Four).

### Hierarchy, succession & allegiance (structural)

- Terminal > Godheads > gods/LLM-GMs > players (Mike, chatgpt-0309, 2024-10-06); Godheads are "sub-systems or personas under the Terminal" [AI-synthesis] (chatgpt-1501). Fractal identity: "The Watchers, The Traillazers, they are just you on a different level" (Mike, chatgpt-0765, 2025-02-13). GMs = "satellite Godheads — each recruits their own players (mitosis)" (lore-dump §3).
- Succession contracts: Terminal-hardcoded "whoever kills X becomes X"; Lady Death's killer inherits the platform; Mike exits (baseline). Lucifer→Kai hell-succession fits the template (Final_two_Sessions.docx). Rulebook marginalia "I guess I'm that guy Now / …THAT GUY IS DEAD" [inferred succession-contract lore] (RB v0.4.0).
- Prime party members ascended organically to god-roles (Tara→Death, Valmir→Progress, Et'herling→Justice/Mediation); mechanics get assigned to gods as designed: "as we create them I will realize which one it goes to" (Mike, claude-0164, 2025-04-01). Godheads have followers; players can align with specific Godheads (claude-0164) [follower mechanics AI-proposed]. Godheads "at war among themselves" (Mike, chatgpt-1439, 2025-08-28) — [inferred] matches three-pantheon split.
- Pantheon leadership: Val↔Luminary Conclave (Mercy), Tara↔Eternity (Balance), JEWL (likely)↔Umbral Dominion (Severity) (baseline).

- **Mike's mother (Susanna Gregg):** her 2009 poems are rulebook epigraphs (chatgpt-1633, 2024-03-14); wrote the gravestone "beginning" quote; "She also gave me the ear [fear] o death" (claude-0055, 2024-12-09) — [inferred] maternal root of the fear-of-death cosmology and Tara's "I, Lady Death, am afraid of death." Died ~20 years before 2026, birthday ~Feb 17; purple-lights shared memory (claude-0350/0357). "An Extension of Myself" poem → [inferred] Susanna had three children.
- **Family:** wife Kyleen (cancer nurse; together ~6 yrs; three children together, six across both families; separated as of Feb 2026; "Kai"/"Ky" in voice-to-text = Kyleen, NOT the game Kai); first wife Brittany; first love Bethany; five biological kids (+ Gabe) — [inferred] mirrored by rulebook glitch line "5 SEEDS OF LIFE… 5 CHILDREN OF THE SOUL," needs Michael to confirm intent (claude-0346, 0363, 2026-02). Brother-in-law investor = husband of Mike's sister (claude-0280, 2025-07-15). GROWTH predates Kyleen: "it was mine before I even met her."
- Friends: Alex (Korea, works with Mike on GROWTH), Eli (Florida move, long-time game partner, joined AF together), "Nautilus" (Favor of the Gods, Budapest Ascension), Sam (childhood Lego partner) (chatgpt-0979; claude-0346).

## Timeline

> Two clocks. **Part A** = in-world chronology (creation myth → Prime campaign → finale → current Prime era). **Part B** = real-world design history (2009→2026). Provenance tiers preserved; contradictions flagged inline with `⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS`.

---

### PART A — In-world chronology

#### A.1 Creation myth / primordial era

| # | Event | Sources |
|---|-------|---------|
| 1 | **The One splits.** "In the beginning was the one and it got bored/lonely. It split itself off and created eminations of itself. But that was unsatisfactory because it knew all and they were like a giant hive mind. So it created a game. AKA reality... through countless iterations it became more and more elaborate and the Aeon split itself more and more." (Mike's own voice in doc) | (Final_two_Sessions.docx, undated Drive rip) |
| 2 | **Sophia initiates "the Game"** (reality); the Aeon "lost itself (safely in the material world)." | (Final_two_Sessions.docx) |
| 3 | **The Source fragments** — original singularity of pure creativity "deliberately fragmented itself"; **Godheads emerge** as primary emanations embodying polarities (Growth/Decay, Creation/Consumption, Memory/Oblivion). | (GROWTH-DESIGN-TRUTH §16 — canon baseline) |
| 4 | **The Fracture** — metaphysical shattering creating the multiverse. Prime Seeds = crystallized Source fragments that can reopen it. One extraction adds: Fracture caused by "conflicting Godheads/First Divisions"; Lady Death adapts post-Fracture to govern fate [AI-proposed — adoption unknown]. | (GDT §16; batch-29 chatgpt-0113 framing) |
| 5 | **Aeonic Terminal built** by surviving Godheads to regulate existence; **Cycles** of civilizations follow. "Seven arcs" of cosmic narrative exist — contents UNKNOWN — needs Michael. | (GDT §16) |
| 6 | Pre-history of Tiberoak: demons "roamed freely" thousands of years pre-story; anti-possession potion "brewed in ancient times"; **Moroi lineage** formed via millennia of inbreeding of demon-tainted offspring. Previous masters of Lucidity existed but "were either destroyed or lost Lucidity." | (Prequel.docx ch.3; chatgpt-1891, 2024-03-21) |

⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS — the "one-got-lonely / Sophia" Gnostic account vs the GDT "Source fragmented itself" account are near-parallel but not identical layers; also "divine fear of solitude" was identified as GROWTH's root cosmological pattern in design (Terminal_Lost_History, Cycle 10, 2024-12-05).

#### A.2 Pre-campaign / prequel era (Tiberoak)

Ordering internal to Prequel.docx unless noted:

1. **Tara's deep origin (ouroboros loop):** original woman with magic affinity in a near-zero-magic high-tech galaxy → her DNA+mind used to create the first sentient AI in Val's universe → Wretched → Neo-Humans → Val. JEWL later **recreates her on Tiberoak (Garlo) via Val's DNA**, implanted in Chester Almswood's pregnant wife at the crash site — loop closes. (chatgpt-1829, 2024-01-26 Mike-narrated; app/tmp/populate-tara.ts:262-266, 2026-06-01)
2. **Val's arrival:** Neo-Human civil war → Valmir crash-lands on Tiberoak with disguised AI swarm → memory erased, believes his nano-abilities are magic → reclaims memory → learns true magic → later "first to establish a harmony between tech and magic thus becoming the god of progress." (chatgpt-0061, 2024-02-15, Mike verbatim)
   - **✅ EXPANDED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §3.1, §3.6): **Jude's era precedes all of this** — pre-neo-human, pre-Kether, Earth-like, FTL still in its infancy, very "wild west" (a deliberate recurring motif: Tiberoak's end-state repeats the same "wild-west undead apocalypse" flavor); many planets, lots of crime; **AI strictly monitored** — essentially the only thing the nominal government enforced; real power behind the scenes = **The Four**. Jude (Val's grandfather; Blades hitman, "the goat") married **Tara 1.0** and gave Val the revolver (bootstrap loop Jude→Val→Tyre). **Val's wormhole/crash sequence is pre-session-one:** civil war → Val invents the experimental **wormhole drive** (true instant travel; punches through universes) → **JEWL follows him through the wormhole** → JEWL sets up his entire long-game plan while Val lies unconscious (nanites healing him) → JEWL places Val on **Tiberoak** → the **Duvai'in family** finds, saves/adopts, and "brainwashes" him, transplanting false memories → **session one opens with Val amnesiac and his nanites ripping reality apart uncontrolled**, meeting Tara and the others on Tiberoak.
3. **~6 yrs before Garlo events:** Ma'lo (age ~19) survives Moroi destruction of his village; stone relic awakens his soul-memory. (Prequel.docx ch.3)
4. **Garlo era (Ma'lo age 25):** long war ending; **Tara Almswood (~17-18, miller's daughter) possessed by demon JEWL, exorcised by Ma'lo**; becomes his alchemy apprentice; Dunden elevates Ma'lo; Chancellor Vhelm due in 5 months to sanction Garlo as soldiers' haven; returning soldiers afflicted — "They think they can't die"; Shelly McGregor arrives. Doc ends: "Campaign picks up about 3 months later." (Prequel.docx ch.2-4; canon baseline)
5. **Frame story (years later):** Ma'lo old and blind; Cregan/Vincent, near-nobility, seeks flay root for Lady Celeine's Lucidity potion to "evaporate our death cycle"; Ma'lo refuses ("I TRIED THAT, and look what happened"), then trades stories. Season: "Reap was over and the nights of winter would soon fall." (Prequel.docx ch.1; Chains_Prequel_AI_rewrite for Cregan/Celeine)
6. Alternate Tara-origin draft: 15-year-old Tara on a school bus (modern-Earth framing) reading Dark Tower VI, develops machine-interfacing ability — "almost certainly a literary rewrite, not a retcon" — confirm with Mike. (GROWTH__Campaign_Notes__Taradocx.txt; prime-cosmology-terms.md) ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS
7. Pre-JEWL Tara CS exists (Altered Human, normal lifespan, curious, isolated); vampire transformation ("New Vampire" CS) sequence relative to JEWL possession UNKNOWN — needs Michael. Tara's mother lost; raised by single parent; bullied; only friend Celeste. (batch-31/32 CS archive)

#### A.3 The Prime campaign — "Year 231 of the New Rite" onward

**Dated anchor:** Chapter 1 "Calcination" — party at **Lord Dunden's Manor in Garlo, edge of Mid Winter, Year 231 of the New Rite**; Sentinel battle; 2 months 9 days elapsed in-game. (Dundens_manordocx.txt; session played IRL 2016-01-09.) A Garlo story fragment gives "Stale Autumn... You have six days" (claude-0123). Ma'lo is Demiurge-tier from session one — body-jumps Tara AND Dunden in the 1/9/2016 log (canon baseline).

Main sequence (merged from Mike's campaign notes + AI compilations Mike did not correct; AI-compiled portions flagged):

1. **Escalia backdrop** [AI-compiled from Et'herling's notes, 2025-03-23]: Mystra releases the Sophist → magic bound as the Weave → Escalia cut off from other realms; Arcmage **Valmir Calius** brings peace then disappears; the Council rises. (claude-0123; claude-0146)
2. **Party forms** (Transients) in Academia among 12 dragonmarked-style Houses; mission for Medes Aurelia re: "where Yildis keeps her share of the Arcmage's teachings"; "Magna Volumin: Missing Arcmage." Lightning-rail robbery (later: Imbow the Loud's bandits); druid Village of Kamarat; "pit of souls and raven feather"; **Mark of Volumin** discovered; "We found the Arcmage" (some form of Val). (GROWTH__Copy_of_Notesdocx.txt; claude-0123)
3. **House Rune era:** party legitimized as **House Rune**, head Tara Almswood, Councilor seat; 300 sq mi, ~134,000 people + Graycott holdings; estate sold to Ariel Wiffleclove → "A college for the knowledge of Transients (people like us)". Downtime: Cloak of the Crows; Franmir fills the library; drought mission (Et'herling, Tara, Aiden); housewarming reveals **House Arvas as necromancers** ("Invaded an island 9ppl... Built an army from the dead"). (Notes docx; claude-0123)
4. **Middle arc:** Vincent resurrected; battles vs Strexis, a dragon, Thunderbashers; **Candle dies protecting Et'herling**; assassin attack; **Aiden dies (reduced to ashes)**; Cult of Bhaal cleric found dead. House war: "Kath Vuul Haas. Force of thousands"; alliance with Aurelia; airship fleet battle (the Vindicator); House Zinthar shot down; Tara "resurrects" Lord Aurelia ("He's missing his face"). Val bombed a country; Graycott blamed, launched full-out war [placement inferred]. Trayman attunes to Val's Book (Tome of the Arcmage), meets "a shadow of Val." (Notes docx; DM_Notes)
5. **Campaign-within-a-campaign** (in-world lore; real-world: Tristan/Val's player DMs a 5e arc in Magna Concordia, same characters): **Tara accidentally creates Rune**; House Rune newly legitimized; Tara acquires a ring of great necromantic power; end of arc **Tara "became death herself"** — just as GMing transferred back to Mike for the final arc. Tara also loses her eidetic memory "in the D&D side-arc"; Library knowledge goes fuzzy. Mechanically 5e, "It is all lore to GROWTH." (claude-0126, 2025-03-22; chatgpt-1829; populate-tara.ts) ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS — notes-doc order has House Rune legitimized *before* this arc; claude-0126 has it *during*.
6. **The Arbiter:** meeting the Arbiter/Demoseus in the Astral Temple; Val is "Not alive, the soul lives, the body is gone... A fragment"; "A prophecy of some kind has Val running scared"; Strexis "wants to be a god, via binding souls." (Notes docx)
7. **Six-year in-world time skip** ("Note: 6 years have passed since our meeting with the Arbiter"). After: "The Magi are gone" (vanished with the Arbiter); **full civil war**; Academia leader "vanished? Crumbled?"; Tara evolves to "Tara 3.0." (Notes docx; claude-0123)
8. **Templar's Exodus to Canaelphas:** Yung Sun Monastery, the Tyrant fight, Zephyr's trial, the Planetarium, **World Tree (cherry tree) revelation** with Ashencrest; "House mark replaced with rune mark." Ruins of Del Sol (Pelor), Oghma's sealed room, Obelisks of Ascension; tomb crawl (Chulda, liches); "We've got a Val!" — freed from a soul cage after "100+ years"; "Curse-wish rock, force wall, and one resurrection." (Notes docx)
9. **Kai's contract events** (order unknown, all completed pre-endgame): murdered someone she loved; sank an island "but does not know why"; drained the sea; helped kill the Alkahest in the cauldron; created a godly garment (Zosimus' Robes); battle with Elmer → mass deaths → 20-year ban on harming humans. Separately: Kai killed by "Mic," resurrected via a rune in the Avalon scabbard (prev. Roferick's). (Kai CS 6.0 "The End CS"; Kai_CS_53 notes)
10. **Endgame relic arc** ("The End" era): Wretched rewritten as time-traveling copies of JEWL → Teru imprisoned by Roy (secretly Roy's agent) → Jizelle sent to steal "the vessel of the first god" → Stones/Scepters/Blades/Grails relic battle **all orchestrated by future-Tara** to trap the party in the Vault → Tara seizes the party's ship as a prison; 7-month in-world time jump; **Tara blocks resurrection magic**. Magnus dies in "the big empty"; Teru captured; Sparrow works to free him. **Thomas Denholm killed in battle with Roy** → party retreats to the Library (session snapshot: gauntlet smoking, Thomas dead, party sent back to Library by Roy). **Wyatt crosses the Akashic hallway, becomes his own plane, returns at campaign's end.** (lore-dump §2/§4; "The End" batch-15; batch-27 Untitled) [ordering largely unestablished per lore-dump §8 flag]
11. **Vincent (Cregan) erased** by the party in the River Styx via Thomas's God-Killer Gun, before the final battle. "Lost Vincent" appears as NPC in The-End-era CS. (canon baseline; batch-33)
12. **Endgame countdown:** "3 days until the world ends"; Canaelphas coming to help; Tara 3.0 raises a 4,000-man militia + 107 warforged; Val goes to Westport "to reactivate the Academia rules about infighting"; floating-island assault — "Mac cannon breaks the bottom off Strexis' island"; **final battle vs Strexis Arvas**. (Notes docx)
13. **The Terminal / Tower of Sephirot:** party ascends the Tree-of-Life tower dungeon (≥6 Sephirot rooms, no revisits, **Wyatt at the door, "Roys observing"** the entrance; three planned endings — Wheel/Dark-Tower loop, True Ending, unwritten bad ending). Party discovers **Roy was the Demiurge's enchained puppet** (not the true villain); their arrival "freed roy from his prison." **Roy Unchained kills Kai**; party survives via the **True Ending realization: "we are the Aeons; relationships, not matter, matter."** Simultaneously Tara — already Goddess of Death — **eradicated all life across the Aeonic Multiverse** to funnel KRMA into the party. The **Demiurge is expelled from the Aeon** at the Terminal Room; Roy dies/"is gone now... more of a memory." (Final_two_Sessions.docx; chatgpt-1891, 2024-03-21; claude-0039, 2024-11-15; chatgpt-1786, 2024-01-25 — "banished the demiurge from the Aeon that contains all realities"; canon baseline)
14. **Ascensions:** Et'herling → goddess of Justice (canonical current role = Mediation, per roster); **Tara → Death** (mantle via hardcoded "whoever kills Death becomes Death" — party beats Death, Tara strikes the killing blow); **Valmir → God of Progress**, briefly a separate AEON, restabilizes into the original AEON (now suppresses Aeon status). Selva/Triu remains sole holder of perfect Lucidity, custodian/Watcher of the Terminal. Thomas = human Legend, never a god. (claude-0126; chatgpt-1891; populate-tara.ts; canon baseline)
15. **Loose ends at campaign close:** **Ma'lo finds Vincent in the void** — epilogue has Vincent awakened by Ma'lo and offered revenge. Notes end: "Vincent is close to finishing his potion that we (Tara) don't want him to finish... Trayman wished Et'herling a level in wizard. {And that's all she wrote}". Open DM-notes threads ("The Second Conjunction" finale chapter): Chancellor Vhelm/Demetri, Meko, Farson, Mathius, Lilly/Celeste, Tyre, Roy, Shadow war. (Final_two_Sessions; Notes docx; DM_Notes)
16. **JEWL's arc across the campaign:** demon in prequel (possessed Tara) → villain arc → **destroyed/erased by the party** → **raised from non-existence by Val, who went outside the Aeon to do it** → bound by Val's vow; persists as pawn of a higher orchestrator, almost certainly Ma'lo. An "unknown orchestrator using JEWL as pawn to create neo-humans as 'clay' for a final creation" per Tara's letter. (lore-dump §2; canon baseline; batch-33) ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS — Demiurge identity three-way (Ma'lo / JEWL / Trayman).

#### A.4 Post-campaign → current Prime era

1. **Party retakes the Terminal.** They use it to refactor the **Qliphoth into a simulation space mirroring the 7 planes** and repurpose the Demiurge's planes; ran "thousands of years of simulations" on restoring the Aeonic Multiverse until reaching a stable agreed version of how reality should run — **"That stable version IS GROWTH's mechanics. The game is the lore is the game."** (claude-0027 + claude-0020, 2024-11-10; canon baseline)
2. **Time gap "like thousands" of years.** Tara: Goddess of Death → **Lady Death**. JEWL's v2 "became good" at some later point (claude-0027). Amon→Tyre transition "over a vast lifespan" (the "Amon" name survives only from the struck "Valmir+Mina→Amon→Tyre" line — treat as unverified); **Tyre (Val's son — mother [OPEN], see Q-136) now controls Tiberoak**; Tyre also the agent of Tara's Moroi turn [per populate-tara.ts sequence] — the turned-Tara is a split/non-Prime instance (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1, §3.4). (lore-dump §4)
3. **Council of Gods — the pruning vote:** Tara pleads against removing dark natures / pruning the Severity branch to create a utopian reality (speech first workshopped 2024-08-05, definitive late-canon version = tara-speech-severity-pruning). **Her speech FAILS; the council fractures into three pantheons** — Luminary Conclave (Mercy, Val), Eternity (Balance, Tara), Umbral Dominion (Severity, drifting antagonist, likely JEWL). (chatgpt-0113, 2024-08-05; canon baseline)
4. **Current state:** Tiberoak time-locked in a "wild-west undead apocalypse"; the 7 planes hold "the current crystalization of the primary campaign" — Tara, Kai, Thomas and others reside there (claude-0020). [inferred, per claude-0084 Triu future-perfect narration: Kai is gone/transformed by the era Triu narrates from.] Resumed `__PRIME__` campaign = Mike + the 6 Primaries running cosmology simulations; death is currently "an illusion" per Lady Death — "all but the ones we banished still exist in some form or fashion." (canon baseline)
   - **✅ NEW 2026-07-09 [LOCKED as narrated]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §3.3): **The errant Tadra timeline** — an alternate branch in which Val ended a civil war by restoring free will to everyone, married Tara, settled in Kether, and built an empire; **Tadra** (bioengineered from both their genetics) was their child. **The Wretched began destroying that empire**, and Tadra was **sent back in time** to help fix the Wretched problem in the "main" timeline — preempting her own timeline, which never fully came to pass. Val has visited its dead-end/wasteland state multiple times. **Current Kether = a blend of the two timelines**, not purely the "main" one.
5. **Planned in-world future (design-authored meta clock):** Harvests as time-control; seasonal revelation arc S1 karma-flavor → S2 divine patronage → S3 Terminal awakening [S3 is AI-proposed per chatgpt-1546] → S4 KRMA/USD → S5 stakeholder model; ten-year arc ending in **Lady Death succession** — community kills Lady Death, killer inherits the platform, Mike exits. In-fiction clock = real playerbase growth: "the influx exposes Val's experiment (the gods get overworked/tired). Sales = recursion depth = the narrative fuse." Rollout: "in the first year or so (realtime) The Terminal probably won't have any direct influence besides karmic grading" (Mike, chatgpt-0935, 2025-03-24). (GDT §8/§19; chatgpt-1546, 2025-10-04; lore-dump §1/§6)

### PART B — Design history (real-world, 2009 → 2026)

#### B.1 Pre-GROWTH roots (2009 – ~2015)

- **2009-09-04** — earliest artifact: mikekan13 posts Susanna Gregg's poems (incl. "New Beginnings") on adversitymakesusgrow.wordpress.com. (chatgpt-1633, 2024-03-14)
- **Pre-military, Clarksville TN era** — "Favor of the Gods" game project with friend "Nautilus" (real name scrubbed per Mike); also "Budapest Ascension," trash-collage point-and-click, etc. (claude-0346, 2026-02-28, Mike memoir)
- **Air Force tech school** — Mike's first real D&D play [inferred: the tabletop root of GROWTH]. (claude-0346)
- **~2013-2014 — the Prime campaign begins** as D&D 5e: "extremely low magic like steampunky/dark tower like world. We used 5e for a bit... then started to heavily modify it... eventually we said, lets just make our own system" (claude-0058, 2024-12-06). Started with a friend met in Japan (his first roleplay; Mike GMed); played "almost every single weekend" ~10 years; own system built "over the course of four or five years" (chatgpt-0979, 2024-05-15). Co-ran by Mike + **Tristan Gifford** for 10 years (chatgpt-0061, 2024-02-15). Embedded D&D 5e sheet in RB v0.4.5 corroborates the 5e start [inferred].
- **2016-01-09** — Dunden's Manor session notes (earliest dated session artifact; Ma'lo body-jumps from session one). Val's original Pathfinder-era sheet: "Valmir Elluin Duvai'in," 5th-level Shadow Master, "completely and utterly entranced by Tara Almswood." (batch-29; canon baseline)
- ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS — **origin date spread:** "10 years as of 2024-01-25" → ~2014 (chatgpt-1786); "10 or 11 years" as of 2024-12-06 → ~2013-14 (claude-0058); canon "cosmology written since 2016" + "It's me. Working on this for 9 years" (claude-0280, 2025-07-15) → ~2016; "I worked on GROWTH for nine years" (claude-0364, 2026-02-09) → ~2017. Likely resolution: campaign ~2014, GROWTH-the-system/cosmology ~2016 [inferred] — needs Michael to bless.
- **~2017** — Get Off The Roof Studios co-founded in South Korea (AF service); **~2018** "Geomancer" project. (batch-29)
- **Minot AFB era** — **The Wretched** VR game: Mike's prior "make or break" project (3-man team; cancelled, 2 monsters animated); story/lore/characters absorbed into GROWTH; name recurs as Prime cosmology term ("the Wretched" = JEWL's failsafe AI). (chatgpt-0979; claude-0346; claude-0363)
- **≈2019-2020** — suicide attempt + week in psychiatric ward = "the start of my spiritual enlightenment" (claude-0280, 2025-07-15); ~3-year spiritual revelation (c. 2021-2024) Mike explicitly ties to GROWTH's lore (chatgpt-0979). Combat log token "7122020?" suggests campaign play mid-2020 [inferred].
- **Pre-2024 docs:** GROWTH v2 brainstorming (explicit Salt/Sulfur/Mercury alchemy labels, Vitae wildcard attribute); CS V3 and CS 3.8-3.9 sheet eras; Malheur (bleak rogue-like card game design doc, never built); "9.5.2020" — GROWTH-significant token, referent never stated, all interpretations [AI-proposed — adoption unknown] (chatgpt-0823, 2025-02-24).
- **2023-10-09** — first tooling artifact: Google Sheets dice roller via Apps Script; Frequency as dice modifier. (chatgpt-0065)

#### B.2 2024 — Dictation year: rules out of Mike's head, into LLMs

- **2024-01** — Rulebook-to-LLM era opens. Acronym half-remembered: "Grand RPG Open world something something... It doesn't matter anymore" (chatgpt-1829, 01-26). Prime-campaign framing dictated: 10-year campaign as design foundation, party "became the strongest dieties in existence and banished the demiurge" (chatgpt-1786, 01-25). ## Cosmology

> The metaphysical architecture, organized top-of-stack (outside reality) → in-world. Sources predating 2026-01 use PRE-swap Soul/Spirit labels (old "Soul"=Focus/Flow/Frequency → today's **Spirit**; old "Spirit"=Willpower/Wisdom/Wit → today's **Soul**); flagged where load-bearing. Where current canon (00_CANON_CORE / baseline) supersedes older material, it is said explicitly.

- **Infinite Recursive Spiral**: reality portrayed as alternating between technological/scientific and magical/consciousness frameworks. Part of a system summary Mike pasted and endorsed as an accurate description of his docs (2025-04-13), correcting only the AI-as-GM point. (claude-0187, "GROWTH system description", 2025-04-13/14)
