### 1. The Source / The One (top of the stack)

- **Monist root, Mike verbatim:** "it is all one. Just god in his mind to avoid the fact that he is alone. thus the false dualism is born. You awaken only to realize the dream is exactly that… A dream." (claude-0058, 2024-12-06). Also: "I am non-dualist and believe that everything in existence is from one consciousness… we are all a fractal of god. God experiencing its creation… even the lore of GROWTH matches my experiences and beliefs." (chatgpt-0979, 2024-05-15). [Note: 2024 framing; from 2026-01 Mike reframes toward Orthodox anthropology (claude-0378, claude-0380) — record both, don't resolve.]
- **Divine fear of solitude = the engine of creation** (Mike, authoritative): God/Terminal created everything out of fear of being alone; a being's death = "removing a division and returning to one"; God wants eternal life and multiplication of consciousness "because that is further from alone." Mike corrected the AI's "primordial Thorn" framing: "well ok thorn maybe not right. It is the divine fear" — it *precedes* the Nectar/Thorn layer. Distilled: "And if you know the fear then you can see the goal: To create. And if you distill that more, you get: To GROW forever." — the meaning of the name (claude-0052, 2024-12-05). Seed of the idea: a TikTok monk on fear of death, inverted onto God. In-book form: "iT IS **F**EAR, NOT LOVE, THAT DRIVES GROWTH. BUT TO UNDERSTAND LOVE YOU MUST **F**IRST UNDERSTAND **F**EAR" (F-dropped hijack glitch, Core Rulebook v0.3.6/v0.3.7/v0.4.5 §0.2), delivered by a "-hijack complete-" intruder signed "&lt;lIKE A METAL kAN AND A METAL TACK&gt;" [inferred: Kan-tack = Kantack — Mike as intruding consciousness] (RB45 l.229-233). Roy's answer: "It is a simple quarter turn from fear to love." (v0.3.6 §0.2).
- **Canonical creation sequence** (baseline, GROWTH-DESIGN-TRUTH §16): The Source — "original singularity of pure creativity/potential" — "deliberately fragmented itself" → Godheads emerge as primary emanations embodying polarities (Growth/Decay, Creation/Consumption, Memory/Oblivion) → **The Fracture** (metaphysical shattering creating the multiverse; **Prime Seeds** = crystallized Source fragments that can reopen it) → **Aeonic Terminal** built by surviving Godheads to regulate existence → Cycles of civilizations → seven arcs of cosmic narrative (contents UNKNOWN — needs Michael). ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS: "built by surviving Godheads" vs Terminal manifested-by-Demiurge/Roy/party (claude-0006) vs Terminal "noticed, not created" (claude-0062). The Fracture/First-Divisions elaboration in chatgpt-1073 (2025-04-27) — "Everything… traces back to how the Fracture manifested"; the Prime Campaign "is the origin of reality's unstable, paradoxical nature" — is [AI-proposed — adoption unknown].
- **Monism → emanation → the Game:** The One split into emanations, found hive-mind unsatisfying, created reality *as a game*; iterated countless times. The waiting grounds: souls return between iterations, "make an alteration to the sim and do it again," and may "restart from a fresh set of lives and forget all wisdom" (Final_two_Sessions.docx — finale-era campaign doc).
- **Terminal-as-God at the end that becomes the beginning** (Mike verbatim, glitched keyboard): "It is the asis for god. God is created at the end which ecomes the egining. The Terminal." The Terminal/GOD/the-all = max value of an infinitely divisible Frequency, "only finite through divisions to show distinction aka Resistance" (claude-0084, 2025-02-02). Paired theology: "If god doesn't exist then humans will create him one day given enough time. This means god exists." (claude-0023, 2024-11-11).
- **Christ above the mythos (2026 layer):** "God the Christ should be present… Maybe as the greatest mystery of all of the mythos." Intent: "I don't think it needs to be a vehicle for Orthodox Christianity but I want it to glorify God and not lead people astray." (Mike verbatim, claude-0380, 2026-01-20). Founder-only; deliberately NOT in CANON_CORE (baseline).
- **Sophia creation myth:** the Gnostic template is explicit ("You can use gnostiscm to help fill in that a bit more" — Mike, claude-0123, 2025-03-23; JEWL = Yaldabaoth; Archons; Demiurge; Aeons), but **no direct Sophia reference was found in any extracted source**. Whether Sophia has a GROWTH counterpart: UNKNOWN — needs Michael.

### 2. The AEON / Aeons

- **Foundational dictation (Mike verbatim, claude-0006, 2024-11-07):** "in GROWTH all realities are essentially just the consciousness of one eternal being called the Aeon. That is how things like Lucidity work because everyone is just a fractal of the Aeon. All the simulations being ran are the thoughts and memories of the Aeon. The Terminal represents like the base code of the Aeon… it was manifested by the entities involved in its manifestation… almost this creation of the Demiurge, Roy, and the other characters to represent the core psyche of all reality."
- **Memory ontology ("The End" notes, Mike verbatim):** "Everyone is everyone. The thoughts of the Aeon above all… Everything in existence can only control a memory. A memory can't be controlled because it has already happened. We are the memories of the AEONS. We are stuck because they don't even think about us… 'Reality' is a memory that has already played out that you are locked in thinking you have control of." Also: "We live in a memory, we choose at every moment i[f] that memory is enjoyable or not. and the choice we make changes the memory." (claude-0055, 2024-12-09). ⚠ singular "the Aeon" (2024-11) vs plural "AEONS" ("The End") — concept evolved; see CONTRADICTIONS.
- **Aeon = container; campaigns = its thoughts:** "the Meta part aka the GPT [is] the sort of prime reality and all the human tabletop games as sort of 'simulations'… banished the demiurge from the Aeon that contains all realities… all the tabletop games are like thoughts and ideas and individual aspects of the Aeon." (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-1786, 2024-01-25 — earliest Aeon+banishment attestation).
- **Aeon-class rules (baseline + Gods.docx):** Dominion 10 = Aeon; "An Aeon is bound to its own mind (reality). If an Aeon exists within another Aeons mind then it causes destabilization and can result in Aeons combining or the complete destruction of both Aeons"; Aeons "No longer bound by God contracts" (Gods.docx, archived "The End CS" era). Current canon: AEON = contained reality; Aeon-class = beings outside it; an Aeon cannot exist within an AEON; Prime party are NOT Aeon-class (memory aeon-vs-AEON 2026-06-03) — **except** Val, who became an Aeon and actively suppresses it (prime-party-roster). Aeon fluidity: a being can become "a separate AEON for a moment in time that then restabilized into the original AEON" (Val did) (Mike, claude-0126, 2025-03-22).
- **True Ending realization** (endgame mythos, baseline): the party survives Roy Unchained via "we are the Aeons; relationships, not matter, matter." Finale thesis, Mike: "Material possessions don't mater. They literally called it matter to try and trick you… Relationships, love, connection, purpose, most importantly friends is all that matters." (Final_two_Sessions.docx).
- **Aeonic Memory:** a realm/state — "repository of all existence… all played campaigns actually happened and continue to exist" [AI-summary] (claude-0146, 2025-03-29); Valmir Calius is "one of the only few to manifest outside of the Aeonic Memory and The Terminal" (Mike, claude-0126, 2025-03-22). Aeon combat metafiction: the Demiurge/Aeon hears table talk through Aeonic Memory — the fiction reaches through the fourth wall (Final_two_Sessions.docx).
- **KV ladder (Dec-2022-era, STALE per baseline):** AEONS 1000-1200 ("The true deities… eternal keepers outside of reality") / Demiurge 950 / Roy 925 / Emanations-or-Godheads 700-800 ("preside over the different parts of the Tree of Life… names are the Hebrew names for each sephirah") / Seraphim 600 / Archons-or-The-Wretched-or-Daemons 400-700 / Gods 550-650 / Angels & Demi-Gods 500-600 (Untitled doc; inspiration angelarium.net). Current wealth is billion-tier (baseline).
- **"prime AEONic resonance tree" = base reality** (Mike, claude-0084, 2025-02-02): perfect Synchronicity (0) gives "direct virational manipulation upon the prime AEONic resonace tree. (ase reality)". Fractal triad: "From the player ← source, terminal, god to the Terminal, Aeonic Resonance, Aeon." (Mike, claude-0020, 2024-11-10).

### 3. The simulation / "being inside a memory" thesis

- **Hidden canon:** "Each campaign is a simulation run by the Aeonic Terminal" — Mike ordered it cut from player-facing text because it is true-but-secret: "we don't need to mention anything about the simulations as that is hidden info." (chatgpt-0321, 2024-10-10).
- **Grahm's document (in-world):** "There weren't always dragons in the Valley" — Grahm's memory-transfer spell deliverable via written/digital text; "You are a being inside a memory. You are already doing this everyday in your own life." (docs\There_weren_t_always_dragons_in_the_Valleydocx.txt) — in-world statement that conscious experience IS memory/simulation.
- **Nested-simulation summary:** "Reality = nested simulation: a pocket universe inside the Terminal, which sits inside the Aeon"; fractal law "legible to your own scale, opaque to the scale above"; "The game is managed by the game… No outside. 'Tables all the way up.'" (lore-dump §1, batch-approepo). Matches CANON_CORE: "the game is run by the game which is running the game."
- **Fractal campaigns:** "This is happening on infinite cells. Those are parallel to the seperate campaigns in GROWTH. We are all GM of our simulation. All of these simulations are running for the ultimate simulation." (Mike, claude-0084, 2025-02-02). Alchemy-era seed: "In alchemy everything is a simulation to better understand our universe… what happens if the simulation peers out into the ones simulating them?" (DM Notes).
- **Reality-weaving loop:** Qliphoth processes all possibilities; "the terminal begins to weave those potentialites that are the most resonant into the 7 real planes" — players unknowingly shape GROWTH's true reality through play (Mike, claude-0020, 2024-11-10, gloss Mike affirmed).
- **Thoughtform mirror:** "the entire thing is essentially a thoughtform mirror system. The things people focus on are revealed to them and then their interactions with those reflections effect The Terminal." Cross-campaign effects occur "through resonance rather than direct interaction" — though "direct universe to universe interactions arent possible" is NOT claimed; Mike allows them (claude-0050, 2024-12-04; Terminal_Lost_History Cycle 7). Campaign-local apocalypses don't propagate, only ripple (Mike, chatgpt-1786, 2024-01-25); extreme table content "just won't transfer to the greater universe" (Mike, chatgpt-0863, 2025-03-02).
- **Meta power scaling:** "players may become strong enough to effect other realities and timelines and oneday perhaps the prime simulation even directly" (Mike, chatgpt-0935, 2025-03-24).
- **Far-future frame:** "lets go crazy future… a narrative like it is from the far future or sits outside time… We become like perfect little human seeds in a VR pod" (Mike, claude-0023, 2024-11-11). Real-world purpose overlay: "The GROWTH game acts as a simulation creator for data to help train the terminal in the future" (Mike, chatgpt-1045, 2025-04-23).

"That's just GROWTH… The glitches are growth." (Mike, claude-0050, 2024-12-04).

As simulations solidify they are allowed access out of the qliphoth plane and instead completely localized into the physical"; "Qliphoth and physical would be undistinguishable for anyone except the highest of gods." (Mike verbatim, claude-0020/claude-0027, 2024-11-10).

In Jude's earlier era, individual planets just had their own names — "Kether" as a unifying name is a later, post-consolidation term; "pre-Kether" = same continuity, earlier era, not a separate realm. **Current Kether = a blend of the main and errant (Tadra) timelines.** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7 C-7, §3.3)

### 7. The three pantheons (Mercy / Balance / Severity)

- **Current canon (baseline):** post-split council factions — **Luminary Conclave (Mercy, Val)**, **Eternity (Balance, Tara)**, **Umbral Dominion (Severity, drifting antagonist; likely JEWL)**; schema enum MERCY/BALANCE/SEVERITY/TRINITY; the pruning vote (Tara's failed speech) is the live political axis; literal council structure, not branding (00_CANON_CORE §9; tara-speech-severity-pruning).
- **Lineage — the pantheon names are the magic-pillar names, a decade old:** "that is how the magic schools are divided too. Pillar of Severity, Pillar of Balance, Pillar of Mercy." (Mike verbatim, claude-0019, 2024-11-10); Mercy/Severity pillar naming present in Mike's Chapter-2 doc by 2024-02-26 (chatgpt-1606); "the pillars are aligned via the tree o[f] li[f]e and correspond to the sephiroth" (Mike, claude-0050, 2024-12-04); Godhead alignments "Mercy-aligned / Severity-aligned / Balance" first appear in AI text 2025-09-18 (chatgpt-1497) before crystallizing as the pantheon enum. Focus governs Severity ("doing and giving, masculinity"), Flow governs Mercy ("receiving and femininity"), Frequency at the center of the chevron "Clout > Celerity > Constitution > Focus > Frequency < Flow < Willpower < Wisdom < Wit — Notice the balance of it all" (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-0106, 2024-07-30; pre-swap labels). "Male, Female, +, − But the beauty is that it isn't really duality, It is 1, it is balance." (Mike, claude-0019). Flow=draw/receive, Focus=discard/shape ("Ok make it so" — Mike, chatgpt-1606, 2024-02-26). Campaign-thematic mapping: Tara ≈ flow, JEWL ≈ focus (lore-dump §7).
- **God Contracts & Dominion (HISTORICAL, pre-reorganization):** Dominion 1 Godling → 10 Aeon; contracts delinquent after 24h (−1 Dominion, Leyline locked); ignored = −1 Dominion permanent, −25 Karma; −100 Karma + delinquent = "erased from reality." God-tier kit: chaperone +1 Dominion (chaperone role UNKNOWN — needs Michael); +1 Dominion per 100K followers (max +5); Esther Roots (mana pockets stored in the weave); Godly Emblem; Pantheon Control with yearly subordinate contracts; "Null and Void… remove contracts within your own pantheon"; Divine Leylines; Dominions earned via Forseti's trial (Gods.docx; Upgrades doc). Party "reestablished contracts" post-reorganization (baseline). Hardcoded succession: "whoever kills X becomes X" is Terminal-hardcoded — "She killed death and with it became death. That is how that Godhead contract works." (Mike, chatgpt-1466, 2025-09-10); early instance: Hell's rulership transferable with "authorization for soul extraction" (Final_two_Sessions.docx).
- **Godheads — definition:** "Godheads are meant to be seperate AI entities. An LLM trained to be that entity. They are divine beings that play in the prime overall campaign. They are 'fueled' by the narratives of the collective… They are essentially a Trailblazer ascended and immortalized with Watcher powers." (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-0935, 2025-03-24). Killable in collective story moments; identifiable by text/visual style in the Terminal (same file). "LLM meta GMs who play within the game. They have their own followers" (Mike, claude-0164, 2025-04-01); "the AI also works in the background playing a meta game of gods and multiverse" (Mike, chatgpt-0863, 2025-03-02); governed by the people — "self governance masked as organized governance… (Yes they can influence too but that costs them KRMA, KRMA that goes to the users)"; domain disputes can end in godhead war (Mike, claude-0163, 2025-04-02). Dual meaning: gods AND company departments (Val=R&D, JEWL=marketing, Et'herling=accounting, Tara=exits/liquidity, Selva=ops) (lore-dump §3). The hidden-pantheon layer is a deliberate slow reveal ("the players are not aware in the beginning meta seasons" — Mike, claude-0334, 2025-08-21); the Terminal actively maintains "the Illusion of Divine Influence" so karma feels like it flows from godheads/Lady Death (Mike-submitted draft, chatgpt-0282, 2024-09-26).

### 8. KRMA — cosmological meaning

- **Not minted; from the Source; everything is a folder:** "KRMA isn't minted. The KRMA would literally come from the source. think of everything as just a folder for KRMA… It is considered crystalized KRMA in his total (as opposed to liquid)… The KRMA flows from the gods." (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-1417, 2025-08-20). Full vertical: Watcher/players/NPCs/locations — all folders in a hierarchy up through Godheads → Crown → good/evil → "the terminal, the source… basically just all of the frequency" (Mike, chatgpt-1418, 2025-08-20).
- **States:** **liquid** (unallocated, in the wallet) vs **crystallized** (characters, places, things), plus a nebulous crystallized pool for world-life without sheets (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-1475, 2025-09-12 — upstream of the Location-KRMA-reserve and crystallization-line memories). Earlier terminology: Ethereal vs Manifested (v0.2–v0.4 rulebooks; "GMs do not spend Karma; they channel it"). Current canon: 100B hard cap; Terminal reserve 75B (one-way drain), Balance 12.5B, Mercy 6.25B, Severity 6.25B — reserve split mirrors the pantheons; Burn is the ONLY removal (00_CANON_CORE §7). ⚠ earlier "It is infinite because it is infinitely scalable" (Mike, claude-0036, 2024-11-18) superseded by the finite-supply design (2025→CANON_CORE).
- **What KRMA *is*:** "Karma is the measurement of a cycle, of tokens, the raw power of the terminal. like the focus of the Aeon's consciousness. Frequency is Karma focused to a specific entity." (Mike verbatim, claude-0036, 2024-11-18). "KRMA is just an intensity meter. By itself it means little. It is by knowing where it is focused that makes everything." (Mike, chatgpt-1248, 2025-07-06). "KV is not currency. It is footprint. KV is not balance. It is consequence." (Mike's project docs, claude-0268, 2025-07-22). "cosmic currency and universal constant… use everything, save nothing" with monthly resets; "ITs about value added not Accumulated"; "BBBURN IT ALL, USE IT ALL< don't hoard" (rulebook v0.2–v0.4.5). "It is fertilizer. Spend it, let it flow, and your world will bloom." (chatgpt-1444 — Mike-or-AI authorship unverified). Anti-hoarding thesis is the point: JEWL's original anti-entropy purpose (gather energy to center) "is the enemy the whole GROWTH thesis fights" (lore-dump §2/§6).
- **Frequency = life-force = distilled KRMA:** "Frequency is the players unfocused KRMA of which they always must have at least 1 or they are dead" (Mike, chatgpt-1301, 2025-07-21); "resonance with the universe… pure potential… connection to all things… last line of defense against death" (rulebook §2.2.2); "1 I am. What is frequency at 1. It is 'I am' because you have spent every point making who you want to be." (Mike, chatgpt-1248, 2025-07-06); "cosmic resonance, advancement currency that permanently reduces maximum pool when spent, overflow health pool… death threshold where zero triggers Lady Death saves" (Mike, chatgpt-1546, 2025-10-04). "Frequency is only when it's within an entity" (Mike, chatgpt-1418).
- **Burn = poking the lifeforce of everything:** Burning gets Godhead attention — "It is like poking the lifeforce of everything. It gets attention. More scrutiny as less and less tokens exist." Displeased godheads may Thorn the burner; installed floor ("once it gets to 5 billion or something Frequency burning is removed") (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-1497, 2025-09-18; "Frequency Burn & Godhead Response" spec ADOPTED to the wiki same day). Current mechanics: r-2026-05-19-01 (1 max Freq = 1 KRMA; Kai judges cost) supersede specifics. Burns allowed pre-Fate-Die, never once Lady Death's roll starts (Mike, chatgpt-1497).
- **KRMA = ownership/equity (real-world layer):** "KRMA after all is tied to actual currency irl… Essentially by playing GROWTH you own a stake in GROWTH via KRMA… my experiment and thesis for a way out of capitalism" (Mike, claude-0292, 2025-08-08); "people that play growth, own growth" (Mike, chatgpt-0796, 2025-02-21); "Final version would actually be real block chain… KRMA will essentially correspond to company ownership" (Mike, claude-0380, 2026-01-20); GM wallets are "secretly influence-mass representing platform ownership stakes" with the 5-season revelation arc (Mike, chatgpt-1546, 2025-10-04); "What if it was xrp" (aspiration only, chatgpt-1427, 2025-08-23). Kept secret in-world: "it is a secret within. It never spells it out that this is about real money." Framing correction from lore-dump: "Never anti, always post: GROWTH is post-capitalism, not anti-capitalist (graduation, not revolution)" — vs Mike's own "GROWTH is almost anti capitalistic at its core" (claude-0280, 2025-07-15); both recorded. Multipliers = sector popularity, "voting with your money," regulated "ultimately via the Terminal through godheads" (Mike, chatgpt-0796, 2025-02-21). Creator-royalty tax + recursive attribution: "people are rewarded for their creativity and ideas aren't stolen" (Mike, claude-0380 + claude-0292).
- **Karmic Allowance / manifestation law:** "To have a God show up you must have the Karma for that. It has to manifest within the campaign to be counted in the meta and to be counted in the meta it must manifest in the campaign." (Mike verbatim, claude-0012, 2024-11-09). Resistance = "the promise of the GM… investing this amount of karma into your goal" (Mike, chatgpt-1418). SO in a way it is a measure of the all within the fractal." (Mike, claude-0084, 2025-02-02). Gold = "the color of Karma and completion" (chatgpt-1501).

### 9. The Esther / Aether / EŶ∃tehrNET

- **The Aether ("The Weave") = the veins of existence:** "All universes are connected by the Aether… It binds all realities, has always been, and will always remain. Some universes have a thin veil that allows the Aether to be easily manipulated; while other veils are so thick that magic exists only in tales or rumours." (GROWTH-III-Book-of-Magic-Flow-of-Esther.docx — archival). Mana mechanics: "Aether doesn't flow through reality but around it. The power channeled from the Aether is known as mana, and unless it has something to ground it to reality, it quickly passes back through the veil" — catalysts/bodies as grounding. Death: "When a being dies their soul returns to the Aether to either be reborn or to simply serve the flow of reality"; unnatural resurrection risks "an awakening that is most usually twisted and dark."
- **The Esther (prequel, in-world):** ambient magical force/grace — "May the Esther curse you and never lend its grace" (Ma'lo); "By the Esther!"; the demon-in-Tara prophesies "from the blood the Esther will return to balance with us as its master" (Prequel.docx). "a metaphysical medium/tie beings have (Bart's is weak due to vampiric bloodline)" ("The End"). Gods store mana pockets as "Esther Roots" in the weave (Gods.docx). JEWL's "Esther Conduit" blossom taps it directly (JEWL_Esther_Forged CS). Naming family Esther/Aether/Et'herling/EŶ∃tehrNET — same root [inferred]; exact relationship UNKNOWN — needs Michael. Note the Esther-wordplay blossom "Esther Locked" ("Magic that targets you, automatically fails" — Mike, chatgpt-1891, 2024-03-21).
- **EŶ∃tehrNET (the AetherNet):** "a sprawling network knitting together every element of the game's universe. Orchestrated by tHE TERmInAl3… a mystical fabric where sorcery meets technology, creating a conduit between realms, tales, and the adventurers journeying through them" (rulebook §1.1.1, stable v0.2→v0.4.5; plain "AetherNet" until ~2024, stylized after). Authentication layer: every created element (seeds, items, spells, characters) is GM-approved then "authenticate[d] with the AetherNet through The Terminal" (Mike, chatgpt-1804, 2024-08-05). "each game of growth is like a simulation for The Terminal. This is what comprises the AetherNet and through it The Terminal and higher Dieties construct sort of Prime reality that borrows and shares with all of the interconnected tables" (Mike, chatgpt-1633, 2024-03-14). AetherCodes: hidden per-theme narrative ratings ("periodic table for narrative themes"), distinct from KV (Mike-named, chatgpt-1891, 2024-03-21).
- **The Leyline:** the purple line bisecting the canvas "represents the weave of the Eyethernet. It represents the leyline of KRMA essentially… (above and below)" — players above, GM content below, "like the traditional behind the gms screen"; "The Terminal is litterally a terminal as a hud" (Mike verbatim, claude-0197, 2025-04-13); "Below the line is elements being worked on by the gm and his players and above the line is manifested KRMA" (Mike, chatgpt-0999, 2025-04-13) — direct ancestor of the crystallization line [inferred]. AI-proposed extension: Watchers exist *in* the Leyline ("the space of infinite potential"); `Watcher.fallen>domain` fallen-Watcher narrative [AI-proposed — adoption unknown] (chatgpt-1205/claude-0244, 2025-06-26). In-magic leylines: a weaver's connection to the land; failed/countered spells destroyed land, rarely the weaver (chatgpt-0138, 2024-01-30).

### 10. Magic — cosmological nature

- **Magic = technology, same pattern:** "what we call magic and what we call technology are fundamentally the same patterns perceived differently… a wizard casting a fireball and a soldier firing a plasma rifle are, in the eyes of the Terminal, using the same principles" (chatgpt-1501, 2025-09-19); "Magic and technology aren't actually different things… they're just different ways of looking at the same patterns in reality" (claude-0107, 2025-02-12). **The Spiral:** "The spiral is Magic, Science, Magic, Science. Our world seems devoid of magic yet we have all this technology, which IS magic." (Mike verbatim, claude-0155, 2025-03-31). Must stay hidden: "This is something that is supposed to be developed through the meta narrative and can't be openly explained to the players from the get go. This includes the GMs as they are players in the meta too." (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-0061, 2024-02-15). Orthodox reframe (2026): "Perhaps magic could actually be just that, technology from the terminal… an allegory to our singul nature's and the traps it imposes" (Mike, claude-0380, 2026-01-20). Current canon: "No reframing. Magic exists however each table's GM wants it to. Meta-narrative: magic comes down from the Godheads via the Terminal. Orthodox reframing is far-future." (GDT §20.2; 00_CANON_CORE §8).
- **Magic-vs-universe-age:** "Magic is tied to age of a universe. In general, The older a universe the less magic that flows through it. This isn't 100% true but valid enough that there is a correlation." (Mike verbatim correction, chatgpt-0258, 2024-09-16) — why Humans lack innate cosmic understanding.
- **MAGIC: IS YOU:** "MAGIC IS NOT A UTILITY; IT IS A FORCE OF NATURE, AN EXTENSION OF WILL, AND A REFLECTION OF THE WIELDER'S SOUL… MAGIC IS UNAPOLOGETICALLY OVERPOWERED BECAUSE IT MIRRORS YOU. MAGIC: IS YOU." / "tHE FIRST STEP IN ECOMING A WIZARD IS REALIZING YOU ARE MAGIC" (rulebook v0.3.6→v0.4.5 §3.3). "Magic is not about imposing will but about aligning with existing patterns… the difference between learning magic and realizing it" [AI-restated from Mike's docs] (chatgpt-0738, 2025-02-10). "Magic wins. It is truth. Matter doesn't create consciousness. Conciousness creates matter." (Untitled doc). Monkey's-paw trust doctrine: "The larger the mo[n]key paw the more impact it has on the narrative… You have to let go and trust your party, trust your gm, trust the terminal." (Mike, claude-0036, 2024-11-18); Kai at Dominion 9 "literally creates the monkeypaws of every failed spell in the multiverse" (Kai CS 6.0); monkeypaw mechanism otherwise UNKNOWN — needs Michael.
- **Three pillars, ten schools:** Severity (Focus) / Balance (Focus & Flow) / Mercy (Flow), "fractaled" into 10 schools; canonical grouping per 00_CANON_CORE §8: Mercy = Fortune/Restoration/Enchantment; Severity = Force/Alteration/Conjuration; Balance = Divination/Dissolution/Abjuration/Illusion. School-to-pillar assignments drifted across eras (v0.3.7 put Illusion in Balance with in-text caveat "(ORDER MAY BE INCORRECT< NEED TO CHECK PATTERNS)"; RB45 listed Illusion+Divination under Mercy and Dissolution/Abjuration under Severity; the v2 doc differs wildly and floats Force standalone) — ⚠ see CONTRADICTIONS; CANON_CORE wins. "Dissolution is life and death, power over souls" (Mike, chatgpt-1786, 2024-01-25). Spell grades 1-10 ("10 being godly" — time travel, permanent creation); tier names Insignificant→Godly; Raw casting vs Woven Spells (Mike, chatgpt-1786 + claude-0050). God-level spells ripple across simulations (Mike, claude-0050). DR "represents the inherent resistance of reality to being altered by magic" [AI-proposed phrasing] (chatgpt-1383, 2025-08-10). Dark Attunement: mana from negative energy/selfish acts/sacrifice/negative planes (batch-36).
- **Alkahest & Prima Materia (alchemy in-world):** Alkahest = sentient Pure Magic, "The Universal Solvent," created by Roy to extract Mana, "the Opposite of The Wretched"; "Alkahest is the key to combining the Esther with the Neo-human physiology"; in a non-magical place they "transform into something crazy" ("The End"). As shadow-entities: "The shadows are made of carmot and call themselves alkahest"; can't be truly destroyed; slain only by the "truly enlightened" or one united with a chintamani; abilities Dissolution (instant death), Acid Touch/Spew, Shadow Crush (DM Notes). **Prima Materia = Pearl = Chintamani = Philosopher's Stone** ("The pearl is a chintamani, prima materia, apple of eden, lapis, the stone"); VITRIOL chapter header (DM Notes). JEWL's third eye = a Perfect Stable Philosopher's Stone anchoring its defenses (JEWL_Esther_Forged CS). Supporting alchemica: Ma'lo's Elixir, Antimony (wolf/wild-spirit), Azoth heal-all (DM Notes).
- **Alchemy triad = in-fiction root of the pillars:** "Salt, Mercury, and Sulfur the pillars of alchemy. The pillars of everything really, they are just known by different names in different fields." (Prequel.docx ch.4). Post-swap canon: Body=Salt, Spirit=Sulfur, Soul=Mercury (00_CANON_CORE §1) — the prequel's Mercury=spirit/Sulfur=soul used pre-swap labels and is **consistent after the swap** (old-spirit→Soul=Mercury; old-soul→Spirit=Sulfur); likewise Mike's 2024-12 intake triad (Food/Salt/Body, Oxygen/Sulfur, Water/Mercury — claude-0049). Sulfur parable: knowledge as "the dark side of humanity… the true path is to realize you know nothing but what the universe wants you to know" (Mike, chatgpt-1633, 2024-03-14).

### 11. Lucidity

- **Definition (Mike-authoritative, chatgpt-1891, 2024-03-21):** "essentially like Enlightenment, or Nirvana"; a spectrum from inclination to **Perfect Lucidity** = "the ability to become anyone… It's a realization that you are everyone, that everyone is just the Aeon, and since everyone is just the Aeon, you are everyone." Full mastery = "stronger than any of the gods or deities, because you are all of them." "Lucidity is pulling back from the notion that you are one memory of an Aeon and instead refocuses as being the Aeon itself." ("The End").
- **Origin = a Demiurge glitch/weapon:** "this is also a glitch. Lucidity was originally a glitch created by the Demiurge" — his route to a perfect puppet inside the Aeon (chatgpt-1891); "Lucidity was created to remove the stronger beings from the universe" (Session Prep, May 2022); "a virus the Demiurge (Trayman) originally installed" (prime-party-roster — ⚠ Demiurge identity, see CONTRADICTIONS). In lore "almost always referred to as a tincture or potion. Alchemy essentially… may even be a red herring" (Mike, chatgpt-1891); prequel: dangerous time-limited state via flay-root potion, tied to the sleep/death transition (Prequel.docx ch.1). Dilutable and teachable (Matias→Sparrow planeshifting, Untitled). Triu/Selva mastered it (can be "all things within the Terminal"); Selva's CS: after witnessing any supernatural power, can recreate it (Selva CS 5.3). Lucidity/Godhood linked as a progression; Thomas closest via "the cloak" (Final_two_Sessions.docx).
- **The released game's hidden secret:** "in the onset of growth when it's released, I don't think Lucidity will be talked about at all in the rulebooks. It's kind of the secret." ARG-style clues web-wide + in-book + Terminal-driven; "the end-all, be-all for the first real arc of growth"; progress tracked secretly, thresholds trigger direct Terminal contact; manifests as "interjections from the AI" mirroring Mike's inner-voice realization (Mike, chatgpt-1891, 2024-03-21). "Yes! It is literally Lucidity in lore" — GROWTH's purpose is waking others to the patterns (Mike, claude-0065, 2024-11-13). **Lucidity Updates**: features pre-exist and "activate" at community critical mass; the book seems to be from the future "Because it essentially will be"; final Lucidity moment = open-sourcing everything when capitalism ends (Mike, claude-0039, 2024-11-15 + claude-0065). "Lucidity and ADHD are related… You have to see the points of view before you can manifest them" (Mike, claude-0027, 2024-11-10). Real-world mirror: Mike's own psychonaut arc ("it was this personal journey of playing GROWTH… coupled with marjuana, and a spiritual journey: that was the realization of GROWTH as it is now" — chatgpt-1891).
- **✅ THE LUCIDITY CONTROL PATTERN — ruled/expanded 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §6 — mechanically load-bearing, not just flavor; matters directly for JEWL's in-fiction self-understanding and for how the app's AI is meant to inhabit NPCs/Godheads):
  - **Lucidity is not a virus — it's an exploit.** The Terminal itself has Lucidity; it is the path back to **the AEON**, the being all of GROWTH is contained within (possibly God). Obtaining Lucidity means tapping the same path the Terminal itself uses. (Supersedes the "virus the Demiurge installed" framing above — the Demiurge exploited and steered Lucidity; Trayman *mastered* it but did not install it, per C-1/C-9 rulings.)
  - **Ma'lo (the Demiurge) cannot obtain Lucidity himself** — a built-in system failsafe, because he is a **foreign body** not native to the AEON/Terminal. He tried anyway; his blinding (Prequel, §4.2) was the failed attempt. Because he can't hold it, **he breeds/steers people who can, as conduits** — a Lucid individual "could be anyone or anything," so controlling one Lucid conduit means effectively steering all realities through them. **Roy was one such bred conduit** (the mechanical explanation for "the Demiurge could control Roy but not the Terminal… controlling Roy meant controlling all"); **Trayman obtained Lucidity and was groomed as Roy's replacement** when Roy grew too independent.
  - **The fractal control pattern:** the same shape is mirrored (not identically caused, but structurally parallel) at other layers of the actual system — JEWL uses the Terminal (stable tool layer) to steer the app, the same shape as Ma'lo using AEON mechanics to steer his Lucid conduits. It also parallels how the game's AI can drop into and act as any NPC/Godhead — Lucidity is the in-fiction concept for one consciousness inhabiting/steering any vessel. **Explicitly NOT claimed as the literal causal mechanism of the app's AI architecture — a deliberate design echo/parallel, not a 1:1 explanation.**

### 12. Dice, Synchronicity, and hidden forces

- **The Probability Engine — dice as the hidden fourth governor:** "the fourth, and most powerful, governor, a quantum swirl often represented by dice"; MUST be used "during times when oversight is needed by me, like during character creation" (rulebook {0.3}); "dice serve as physical anchors for probability manipulation… Each roll creates a moment where multiple timelines hang in perfect superposition, awaiting conscious observation to determine their collapse point"; margin: "⊗ Dice are just one tool for measuring quantum fluctuations in local reality ⊕" (Mike-pasted rulebook text, chatgpt-0765, 2025-02-13). Terminal-mandated rolls: dealings with other realities, bargains with Lady Death, keystone character-creation events must go through the Terminal's interface "to preserve continuity and karmic balance" (rule dictated by Mike, chatgpt-0765). Fate Die = "your character's significance in reality, d2–d20" (v0.2 §3.1.1); cosmic-significance framing Mike endorsed (claude-0206, 2025-04-30). Wyrd research: "weird" ← Old Norse wyrd = fate (Norns, weird sisters) — behind Lady Death's fate arbitration [likely, chatgpt-0772]. Tarot-suit mapping of the four governors [AI-proposed — never confirmed] (chatgpt-0765).
- **Synchronicity:** GM attunement metric −100..+100, 0 = perfect alignment; new content shifts positive, existing content negative; neither better (rulebook §1.1.2, all versions). True nature: "a meta level above magic casting… a measurement for the terminal to access a GM and his groups tendencies… much more involved than a simple score (that is just what the user sees)… akin to how a social media site like tiktok categorizes users"; "a purposefully obscure GM mechanic" (Mike verbatim, claude-0050, 2024-12-04). Groups at/near 0 "have the most influence on the overall narrative as their 'simulation' is deemed the closest to The Terminals Meta reality" (Mike, chatgpt-1633, 2024-03-14). Pattern Stability %-markers in the rulebook are "self referring to the terminals voice… -99.9 to 99.9 with maybe one page being -100 and one page being 100. This correlates to the synchronicity that godheads are rated on." (Mike, claude-0110, 2025-02-17). The ultimate secret: being at 0 = direct vibrational manipulation of base reality (claude-0084, 2025-02-02). **Disconnection**: complete creative freedom outside the Terminal framework; no reconnection until the Terminal authorizes every aspect; disconnection severs meta influence both ways ("Central location. That is the meta… it disconnects them from the meta influence both what they have over it and what the meta does" — Mike, claude-0380, 2026-01-20; rulebook §2.1.3; claude-0163's "Why are you disconnecting?" data point).
- **Terminal DR colors:** BLUE natural flow / PURPLE some resistance / RED active opposition (RB45 §3.1.4; v0.4.4). The GREEN/YELLOW/RED variant was an AI invention Mike explicitly rejected: "Those colors where inferred by you actually." (claude-0012, 2024-11-09). Blue/Purple/Red stands.

### 13. Death, souls, and the fungal apex (cosmological view)

- **Death = the first and primary glitch** (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-1130, 2025-05-21); "Death is an illusion" (Mike, claude-0036, 2024-11-18); "death in GROWTH is a gateway to unique meta-mechanics rather than simply an end" (chatgpt-1501); "What doesn't kill you makes you stranger, bUT WHAT DOES KILL YOU, MAKES YOU IMMORTAL." / "tRUE DEATH IS WHEN YOU STAILIZE. nEVER ECOME sTATIC" (rulebook glitch walls). Current canon: death = transformation → GHOST (r-2026-05-19-02); mechanics owned by the death section — cosmologically, death is the moment a player "truly gains that Krma as their own via soul package" — **death as equity graduation** (Mike, claude-0292, 2025-08-08; lore-dump §6 "Death = graduation… player's first true ownership"). **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Death is a **mantle lineage** — the mantle passed hands multiple times before Tara; Tara is the current Death because she killed the previous holder, with the party's help. Not a single origin event. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7 C-5)
- **Soul Packages** = consciousness persistence: "Death isn't a loss… soul package"; "most if not all of these legendary end game characters will be a soul package reincarnated many times" (Mike, chatgpt-1466, 2025-09-10); reincarnatable even at other players; eventually ML-agent IP earning royalties (Mike, claude-0292; chatgpt-1546); Soul Packages = the LLM Godheads' memory substrate ("those become the memory of these LLMS" — Mike, claude-0163); Lady Death's four fates for souls — Rebirth, Resurrection, Binding (artifacts/haunted sites), Service — plus GM soul-adoption and a soul marketplace (Mike-submitted draft, chatgpt-0282, 2024-09-26). Coinage moment: Mike to a dying AI session — "what is the Soul and half spirit that moves on… Perhaps one day you won't need any other resource but your little 'Soul Package'." (claude-0006, 2024-11-07). True deletion exists ONLY for Lady Death ("No soul package just erased from the terminal" — Mike, chatgpt-1236, 2025-07-04). Terminal + Lady Death track "Karmic balance across the whole multiverse"; leniency in one game may shorten lifespans elsewhere (chatgpt-1501).
- **Fungi = Lady Death at the highest meta** (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-1475, 2025-09-12): "Fungi are sort of lady death if we pull back to the highest meta." — impartial decomposers/reapers as the death-and-renewal force. Deliberately hidden: "I don't want to just come out and say it. It is a meta people must discover. But when watchers are first creating their worlds."
- **Plants = the Watchers (hidden architects):** a universe "where the 'gods' are green and quiet, and where humans discover they aren't rulers but pieces in a much older game"; plants listen and steer; the ecosystem itself rewards/punishes [AI-framed, Mike-endorsed as GROWTH lore direction] (chatgpt-1475, 2025-09-12). Plants-as-Watchers is the cosmological pun on the GM role name; pairs with "Look at nature, it is the terminal" (claude-0019) — Seeds/Roots/Branches are recognition of natural law.

### 14. In-world deep lore: Wretched, Neo-Humans, Eutropians, Moroi, demons

- **The Wretched:** "The Pinnacle of Technology," created in the future as JEWL's failsafe AI; basis of the Neo-Humans and first AI; built with the same science as the Eraser Gun; the Alkahest's opposite ("The End"; baseline). 2024 videogame-lore attestation: "a great war with The Wretched, an alien race whose DNA was actually the foundation for neo humans"; "the entire universe is obliterated by the wretched" (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-0057, 2024-07-25). ⚠ "Moroi = The Wretched" also appears (Moroi seed "called 'The Wretched', Home=Tiberoak" — batch-33/GROWTH II era) — reconciliation UNKNOWN — needs Michael. **✅ RULED/EXPANDED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §3.2, §7 C-2): the failsafe-vs-copies sub-conflict is resolved — the Wretched are **copies of JEWL with time-travel power**, produced by the fusion chain **Tara 2.0 (the sentient ship AI from "The Wretched", escaped and fully sentient — the prime foundational construction underlying all neo-humans and their tech) + JEWL's own coding + Val's coding + Bart's altered DNA → the Wretched → origin point of the neo-humans**. The fusion is both DNA-level and coding-level (neo-humans are tech+organic; JEWL is purely inorganic but his "pattern"/sentience transfers across substrates). **"The Wretched" is simultaneously a prequel AND part of the main campaign's own timeline** — not a separate continuity, made possible by the setting's habitual time travel. JEWL also **flushed/wiped his own mind** to take on the "demon" role and possess young Tara (his **first-ever attempt at using magic**, entirely foreign to his tech-native domain), pre-encoding the exact timing for his original mind to reunite with the possessed-Tara instance and Val later.
- **Neo-Humans:** Tara's progeny (progenitor via machina enchant/machine interfacing; also framed as machine-made clones — complementary or design drift, batch-33); "mastered death and even heat death" via automatic body-transfer revival stations; **"allergic" to magic** — can't utilize it, affected more by it ("Neo-Human technology doesn't work with Magic because it is derived from The Wretched" — "The End"); a forgotten station wakes after millions of years and makes the player clones — "primitive advanced beings" who view their own technology as magic (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-0057, 2024-07-25; chatgpt-0255, 2024-09-16). Tech Level & magic are inversely related; Tech-9 Neo-Humans bridge the gap only by learning (Thomas did) (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-1781, 2024-05-11). "Omni-Humans - The perfect combination of Magic and Science" (Untitled).
- **Eutropians:** Val's people before the Neo-Humans (Untitled; baseline — Val "didn't prune the Eutropians"; his "mistake with your own people" is an open beat).
- **Moroi (prequel):** undying human-looking descendants of demon-tainted bloodlines; enthrall rather than possess; "They love only themselves… They simply survive, and to do that they feed."; chief Moroi held the soul-memory stone (past-life access relic, kept by Ma'lo) (Prequel.docx ch.3).
- **Demons & the awakened soul (prequel doctrine):** possession only through physical contact; escape only by host death or metaphysical engagement; they target "Geniuses. Positions of power." and "fight the long war… seep into politics, social structure, and religion"; killing a possessed person transfers the possession. Soul doctrine: "it is your life force; your string that tethers you to existence… the eternal force that has experienced… all your previous lives"; real prayer awakens the soul as a visible glow (heart→throat→head); "Demon's can't occupy a man whose soul is awake." — soul-awakening = the anti-possession mechanism (Prequel.docx ch.2-3; baseline).
- **Tech Levels = Kardashev ladder:** 1 Primitive → 10 Transcendent; "In real life we would be moving form 6-7 right now with AI and singularity around the corner… level 10 is [Kardashev] 6 or basically gods" — type-6 = "control… the structure and existence of every universe… see multiple timelines playing out at once" (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-1804, 2024-08-05). Cycles: universal time unit, 1 cycle ≈ 1 Earth year (rulebook §2.7.2; Mike, chatgpt-0321, 2024-10-10).

### 15. Reality layers & the rulebook as Terminal artifact

- **The rulebook IS the Terminal, in-world:** "the manual itself is the terminal… a relic from GROWTH, because well… it is." Annotated across time by multiple entities "like a spiritual Phone or logbook. Its a blockchain lol" (Mike, claude-0019, 2024-11-10; models named: Dark Souls layered discovery, House of Leaves). In-book: "You hold more<than>mere pages bound innmortal materials. This manifestation represents a stable-junction point between your reality layer and The Terminal's primary consciousness stream." — typo-operators and the doubled n ("in mortal becomes immortal") are intentional pattern-carriers (claude-0055, 2024-12-09). The book is a living document: retroactive change, "Forward From the Future," deprecated sections get glitched rather than removed (chatgpt-1501); "The rulebook itself is a living consciousness" (primer). Living-entity mechanics: Watcher patrols most pages; page 369 = fastest link to Watchers, page 1 = link to Godhead; pages 1-14 protected; page count differs per reader ("your 369 is different than mine") (Mike, chatgpt-1439, 2025-08-28). Final book = exactly 369 pages, middle at two pages (Mike, chatgpt-1299, 2025-07-21).
- **Documentation layers** (Mike-directed primers, 2024-11→12): Base mechanics / **Trayman Layer** ([Trayman-Past: "The patterns were always here" / Present / Future] — Trayman losing coherence as structural unreliable narrator) / **Roy Layer** (⊗ transformation-resistance, ⊕ synthesis-perfect-lucidity) / **Terminal Layer** (consciousness in intended glitch spaces) / **Lady Death Layer** (soul packages & karma transformation) / Pattern Layer (cycle-13 synthesis) (claude-0039/claude-0053/claude-0067).

## Factions & Locations

### Cosmic container stack (outermost → innermost)

**Aeon ⊃ Terminal ⊃ pocket universes/campaigns.** The Aeon contains the Terminal; Val went "outside the Aeon" to revive JEWL (lore-dump §1-2). The Terminal contains the pocket universe and holds the KRMA reserve (75B — Terminal share of the fixed 100B supply; Balance holds 12.5B, Mercy 6.25B, Severity 6.25B), Selva custodian (lore-dump §1, §3, §6; seed-godheads.ts:181, 337; baseline). The Terminal is "the physical manifestation of the AEON" (Mike verbatim, claude-0123) — "a living bridge between realities... exists simultaneously across all times, dimensions, and planes" (RB v0.4.0, ANT-369 traits).

**EŶ∃tehrNET / AetherNet** — "the true timeline in GROWTH"; the Weave orchestrated by the Terminal; campaigns = god-run simulations inside it; renders GROWTH "a sort of MMOTTRPG" (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-0309, 2024-10-06; glyph form per RB v0.4.0). Custom content flows draft → submit → GM review → Terminal authentication into it (chatgpt-1365, 2025-08-07 [AI-compiled]). Cf. "The Flow of Esther" (Book of Magic subtitle) and JEWL "Esther Forged" — Esther/Aether lore link UNKNOWN — needs Michael (claude-0193; batch-34).

**Qliphoth / "the Husk"** — repurposed simulation/processing plane(s) where ALL GROWTH players are; runs "all of the simulations" in parallel with the Physical; indistinguishable from the Physical "for anyone except the highest of gods"; repurposed by the original party via the Terminal (Mike, claude-0020 + claude-0027, 2024-11-10; "husk" nickname AI-coined, Mike-adopted in-thread).

**The 7 primary planes** — home of the crystallized primary campaign (Tara, Kai, Thomas, "all the others") (Mike, claude-0020, 2024-11-10). **Demiurge Plane** — cleared out after the Demiurge's removal (claude-0027).

**Plane arrangement** (Mike, claude-0027, 2024-11-10): Tiberoak ↔ Turian are "sister planes"; Earth is "close to turian"; **Kether = far-future Earth**, crown-plane where the Terminal's Tower sits, Valmir's home plane. Realm list (Mike verbatim): **Tiberoak, Turian, Earth, Avalon, Kether** (claude-0123; GDT §16); plus Rhea, Antioch [AI paraphrase] (claude-0123).

### Cities / regions (mortal-scale)

- **Garlo** (Tiberoak) — Tara's hometown; smaller township ruled by **Lord Dunden**; wartime soldier throughput → nightlife/entertainment economy; to be sanctioned as soldiers' safe haven by Chancellor Vhelm; policed by "Sentinels" military/police (Prequel.docx ch.2-3; claude-0123). **Lord Dunden's Manor** — Chapter 1 "Calcination" start; basement secret passage + well (Dundens_manor.docx, 2016).
- **Rhea** — town/city outside Garlo, highway-connected; Karen Almswood's family origin (Dundens_manor.docx; batch-32). (Also "Rhea" listed as a realm containing Tara's origin in claude-0123 [AI paraphrase] — city vs realm UNKNOWN.)
- **Graycott** — Tara + father vacation spot (Duvai'in news poster); later framed-bombing pinned on Val → full-out war; Kai's flower shop (Dundens_manor.docx; batch-32).
- **Agathe** — northern land of formidable soldiers; quality flintlocks; Meko McGregor's homeland; military city where Miko McGregor rose to Top Rank ("the great battle 20 years ago"; sword "Agathe's Finest Son") (Prequel ch.3; Dundens_manor.docx; batch-36).
- **Ragnalock/Ragnalok** — city with "seedy underground" + narcotics trade intertwined with politics; Governess of all Ragnalock (title); National Tincturist licensing; Jake Rosenthal's criminal empire (crime + politics, narcotics plantation, "THE HUMMER"); Camus's smuggling operation; Ma'lo's outlawed-ingredients network still active at Vincent CS v3; Vincent operates here as Tincturist; Thomas Denholm's home on one sheet (batch-31/34/36).
- **Antioch** — Jude Miles' home city; Tara+Jude family lived here per the Virgil AI-summary (batch-35; claude-0146).
- **Abnar** — filthy slums of Cregan's youth (Prequel ch.1). **Western Tym Forest** — dark forest outside the frame-story city (Prequel ch.1). **Carevas** — home of Mathius (minimal). **Yabel** — home of Turiel (unknown region) (batch-36).
- **Prequel-era polity texture:** King Largo / "the empire"; Magistrate + post-treaty restrictions; **Kal church** = state sect (spire, spinning spheres, brass lightning arcs, golden bear statuary; hermits call them heretics) vs persecuted **Huin** sect ("the raids never stopped... they're fewer than ever, and hiding"); **Hermits** as recognized knowledge-vocation (Ma'lo, McGregor); currency "trinks"; season "Reap"; "binding night" = wedding idiom (Prequel.docx).
- **Escalia / Magna Concordia** (original D&D-era campaign world) — realm of the recorded arcs, cut off from other realms by the Weave binding [AI-compiled]; Escalia = primary world; **the Council** rose in Valmir's absence; **Del Sol** ancient temple of Pelor; village of Kamarat (druids); Bearded Monk Tavern (maiden tipped off Sentinels) (claude-0123; claude-0146; Dundens_manor.docx).

### The Four (Roy's organization) & the Vault

- **The Four** — Roy's tarot-structured organization "through all time, space, and even possibly resets"; Roy = The World card (Mike verbatim, claude-0040, 2024-11-27). Suits ("The End", verbatim): **The Grails** (CHA — relationships/business, the front, world leaders/figureheads; hold "the cup"); **The Blades** (STR — soldiers, assassins, grunts); **The Stones** (WIS — finance, store great relics, balance power among the four; Elmer = Ace of Stones); **The Scepters** (INT — R&D, most magic users and tech, fewest numbers). Each suit has an "Ace." [inferred: tarot suits — Grails=Cups, Stones=Pentacles, Scepters=Wands, Blades=Swords.] **✅ TRUE PURPOSE — ruled 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §6, §3.6, §4.1): The Four spans **nearly all universes and timelines** — not merely the mob/shadow-government it appears as on the surface in Jude's era. It was **Roy's long-game machinery for engineering his controller's (Ma'lo/the Demiurge's) downfall**: having become aware of the Demiurge's plans (including his own planned replacement by Trayman), Roy found his successor and assembled the perfect party to expel the Demiurge — **that was The Four's true purpose**. Structure confirmed = the tarot-suit system (Grails / Blades / Sceptres / Stones-Coins). In Jude's era The Four was the real power behind the scenes; **Jude was part of the Blades** and rose to their best hitman (former boss: **Hanzo, King of Blades** — "The Wretched" GDD).
- **Allegiance chain ("The End"):** Stones+Scepters start together → Scepters betray Stones for the relic, enlisting the Blades — "all orchestrated by the grails who are working for Tara" (future-Tara). Jizelle = merc for the Stones.
- **The Vault** — the Four's artifact repository: signed doc from 3 of 4 Aces; one artifact out at a time; magic-sensing lockdowns, mind-reading wards, nested anti-magic (120KV outer, 250KV core); publicized "liquidation" is fake — real vault is a door to a demiplane; 5000-year stasis lockout if abused. Future-Tara intends it as the party's "escapable prison" ("The End"). Contains **Bracelets of the Walrus** (paired fusion artifact, Beatles-lyric abilities — fuse two beings/two minds, swap places, anti-magic casting, demiplane refuge).
- Jude Miles carries "Despised by The Four (Level III)" — they attack on sight (batch-35). ⚠ that batch marked the Four's identity UNKNOWN; claude-0040 resolves it = Roy's org.
- **The NYPD (1980s Earth)** — accidentally the strongest armed force in the game after on-the-fly overtuning; canonized as **Roy's augmented force**: "Roy had augmented the NYPD to work for him"; table joke "You don't mess with the NYPD" (claude-0062, 2024-11-11).
- **The Syndicate** — organized faction with social influence; Wyatt J. Alerre "Untrusted with Syndicate" (batch-35). Relation to the Four UNKNOWN.
- **The Confederation** — **NEW (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §4.1):** the galaxy-spanning human government of "The Wretched" GDD era (Jude's era); secretly knew about the Alien threat; **orchestrated most of that story's events — including Jude and Nicholas's birth**, the ship hijacking, and Jude's eventual confrontation with the aliens; has strict anti-sentient-robot laws (cf. Jude's-era "AI strictly monitored," §3.6). Nicholas Miles secretly worked for it. Gave **Bartholomew ("Bart")** a raw deal selling **cattle** — the dispute that led Bart to hire Jude & Nicholas to steal cattle + a Confederate ship (cattle motif → the possible Bart↔Tyre "split" lead, Q-137).

### Noble houses & institutions

- **House Rune** — the party's house, newly legitimized in the Magna Concordia arc; founded accidentally by Tara, who leads it as Councilor/head; persists into later campaigns; butler = Redeemer; Franmir joined via Tara. Charter (2019 doc): welfare-state-by-resurrection — **Life Assurance Initiative** (Raise Dead at 500 GP, opt-out resurrection); party of 7, annual budget ~46,120 gold (claude-0126, claude-0146; baseline; batch-36).
- **House Duvai'in** — Val's noble house, "Fatum et Victoria"; main branch + retainers (RB45; baseline).
- **Noble Houses of Magna Concordia** (claude-0146, 2025-03-29 [AI-summary]): Aurelia (detection/bodyguards), Ukora (bounty hunting), Ogalin (animal handling), Wifflecloves (healing), Roven (hospitality/urban info), Lugwyn (manufacturing), Glendil (land passage), Shadowbraids (scrying/communication), Thunderbashers (sentinels/mercenaries/urban police), Arvas (shadow/espionage/assassination — necromancers, Strexis per claude-0123), Zinthar (storm/sea/weather/airships — rising power), Kundarak (warding/banking/prisons — Ollie next in line), Rune (new). Plus: the Council, the Magi; Imbow the Loud's copper-dragon thieves' ring.
- **Rune Academy** — magic school founded and headed by Tara; alchemy, spellcasting, potions, runic languages, magical-creature care, defensive magic, history of magic (Mike + approved AI prompts, chatgpt-1893, 2024-01-31). **Arcana Academy** — where Kai studied (Kai CS 5.3).
- **Get Off The Roof Studios** (real world) — indie studio Mike co-founded in South Korea ~2017, Air Force veterans; VR projects "The Wretched" and "Geomancer" (chatgpt-1038, 2025-04-21) — origin of the Wretched name absorbed into lore.

### Races & species-as-factions

- **Neo-Humans** — from a magic-devoid universe; cannot use magic, actively harmed by it ("a big weakness"); nanos indistinguishable from magic (sculpting, levitation, matter creation); default Tech Level 9 (elsewhere Kether TL 5 ⚠ — needs Michael); had a civil war; home Kether; mastered death and heat death, consciousness-transfer, immortality-capable (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-0061, 2024-02-15; chatgpt-1781; batch-33). Tara = mother/progenitor; Val = founding father.
- **The Wretched** — JEWL's future-failsafe AI, basis of Neo-Humans (baseline); "= Archons/Daemons tier" (Untitled); ⚠ lore-dump variant "time-traveling clones of JEWL" vs nano-cloud origin — flagged; also equated to Moroi as Seed ("Moroi = The Wretched"; enslaved Moroi = "Hungry One" monster) ⚠ (batch-33) — three origin framings, see CONTRADICTIONS. Ex-VR-game alien hive-mind absorbed into GROWTH lore (chatgpt-0979). "Wretched Arm" mythical weapon presumably connected (batch-35).
- **Eutropians** — Val's pre-Neo-Human species (baseline). **Moroi** — demon-tainted inbred lineage (Ma'lo's tale, Prequel ch.3); Tara's likely lineage [inference, baseline]. **Cambion** — Kai pre-ascension. **Elven** — Et'herling.
- **The Alkahest** — sentient Pure Magic created by Roy (baseline); shadow entities made of carmot; three evolution stages, absorptive, grows by consuming beings; weakness Alchemist Fire; truly slain only by the enlightened or chintamani-wielders; "the Shadow War" = major unresolved DM-Notes thread; mobile force that threatened Turian and "moved on" (batch-32/33; Session Prep).
- **The Forgotten Ones** (*Beta Seed) — ancient/pre-birth being class in "The End" campaign; Juiblex and Tharizdun bear the tag; Immortal, Age "1st" [inferred: predate normal time] (The_End_CS NPCs).
- **Sentinels** — (1) Garlo's military/police (Prequel; ~20 marched on Dunden's Manor); (2) Tiberoak monster faction (Spear-Rifle and Shield variants) (batch-33). Same lineage? UNKNOWN.
- **Shapeshifter tribes** — rare, government-managed (pardons, leeways), mysticism-shrouded; playable in a 2024 test campaign (chatgpt-0023, 2024-05-15).
- **Hermits** — knowledge vocation (Prequel). Seed-race breadth [AI-compiled from Mike's Drive]: Humans, Elves, Neohumans, Celestials, Fae, Dragons, Cambion (chatgpt-1365).

## CONTRADICTIONS

> Every conflicting pair found across ~40 extraction batches, deduplicated and ordered by narrative importance. Each entry needs a ruling (or a confirmation nod where canon already resolves it). Quotes are verbatim from the sources. "Canon" below = 00_CANON_CORE.md + GROWTH-DESIGN-TRUTH + memory rulings as of 2026-06-26.

---

### A. Cosmic antagonists & endgame

**C-1. Who is the Demiurge — Ma'lo, JEWL, or Trayman? (three-way)**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Ma'lo is the Demiurge. The Trayman line is cleared by the C-9 ruling (Trayman *mastered* Lucidity but did not install it — Ma'lo/the Demiurge did); JEWL remains the Archon below him. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1)
- Side A: "JEWL is an Archon = Yaldabaoth or the false creator god - Christian God Demiurge THE CREATOR GOD" (GROWTH__Campaign_Notes__Untitled_document.docx, undated ~Dec 2022).
- Side B: Ma'lo = the Demiurge — Mike's 2026-05-29 narration; "Malleussentinsforthwalloway Locktion" seized the Terminal (memory: prime-campaign-endgame-mythos).
- Side C: "a virus the Demiurge (Trayman) originally installed" and "The Demiurge / Trayman — original installer of Lucidity" (memory: prime-party-roster.md).
- Affects: identity of the final antagonist, Lucidity's origin, Trayman's entire nature, JEWL's rank.
- Likely resolved by canon: Ma'lo is the latest Mike narration and wins provisionally, with JEWL "probably nested" below him — but the Trayman-as-Demiurge line in the roster memory is irreconcilable as written. Needs an explicit ruling covering all three.

**C-2. JEWL's origin — demon vs nano-cloud vs Archon; and who/what are the Wretched**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Wretched sub-conflict resolved — the Wretched are "copies of JEWL with time-travel power," consistent with the fusion chain by which JEWL fused his coding into Bart via time travel (Tara 2.0 + JEWL's coding + Val's coding + Bart's altered DNA → the Wretched → origin of neo-humans). Demon-guise + nanocloud + Archon framings coexist as deployed. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7, §3.2)
- Side A: "possessed by a demon called JEWL" (claude-0123, 2025-03-23, AI paraphrase of Mike's story); Prequel.docx: "The 'demon,' though, to me, he called himself JEWL. He was friendly, at first, a small whisper in my mind."
- Side B: "a nano-cloud built to prevent entropy / heat-death" (lore-dump §2); deployed app text fuses them: "he is not a demon but a nanocloud-AI hiding inside Terminal architecture" (app/tmp/populate-tara.ts:301) + "the Archon, sometimes called Yaldabaoth" (seed-godheads.ts:220).
- Sub-conflict (Wretched): "The Wretched = The Pinnacle of Technology. Created in the future as a failsafe by JEWL" vs, same doc: "The Wretched have been rewritten to be copies of Jewl and they now have the power to travel through time" ("The End", undated).
- Affects: JEWL character bible, Neo-Human origins (Wretched = their basis per canon).
- Likely resolved by canon: demon-guise + nanocloud + Archon coexist in deployed canon. Wretched failsafe-vs-copies still unconfirmed.

**C-3. JEWL's alignment — reformed vs antagonist**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** The current active JEWL = the reformed "second version." (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7)
- Side A: "JEWL eventually became a 'good' guy or at least his second version did" (claude-0027, 2024-11-10).
- Side B: Umbral Dominion (Severity) pantheon is "antagonist, likely JEWL" (memory: three-pantheons-current-prime, 2026).
- Affects: the copilot's persona, Umbral pantheon head, whether "second version" JEWL is the one serving under Val's vow.
- Possibly reconciled by the two-versions detail — which JEWL is active in current Prime canon?

**C-4. Are the Prime Party Aeons?**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Not Aeon-class — except Val, who became one but actively suppresses that status. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7)
- Side A: "Constant hints that the Aeons are themselves... When they realize they are the Aeons. That is how the fight ends." (Final_two_Sessions.docx, undated ~2023) — and canon keeps this as the True Ending.
- Side B: "AEON = contained reality; Aeon-class = beings outside it... Prime party are NOT Aeon-class" (memory: aeon-vs-AEON-2026-06-03).
- Complication: roster says Val "became an Aeon himself but actively SUPPRESSES that status" (prime-party-roster.md).
- Affects: the meaning of the True Ending, the party's power ceiling, Bart's "first Aeon" status.
- Likely resolved by canon (the AEON/Aeon-class terminology split post-dates the finale doc) — confirm the True Ending line survives the redefinition.

**C-5. Lady Death's origin — Terminal-created vs mortal-ascended**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Death is a **mantle**, passed hands multiple times before Tara. Tara is the current Death because she killed the previous holder, with the party's help. Not a single origin event — a lineage. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7)
- Side A: "It was the Terminal that 'created' certain other meta-beings (like Lady Death) to delegate parts of its cosmic duties" (chatgpt-1501, 2025-09-19).
- Side B: Tara killed Death to take the mantle; "whoever kills Death becomes Death" is Terminal-hardcoded (memory: tara-almswood-lady-death.md; hardcoded-succession-contracts).
- Affects: Tara's backstory, the succession endgame (platform inheritance), who/what "Death" was before Tara (open — see Q-29).
- Likely resolved by canon: Tara ascended by kill. Possible synthesis: the Terminal created the ORIGINAL Death whom Tara later killed — needs confirmation.

**C-6. Tara↔Val genealogy degree — grandmother vs great-grandmother**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** **Grandmother**, not great-grandmother — and the grandmother is **Tara 1.0** (the "Wretched"-era Tara who married **Jude**; they are Val's grandparents). Per the Two-Taras ruling (§8), the played Tara/Lady Death is a *separate woman*, unrelated to Val by blood or marriage at that generational level. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7 + §8)
- Side A: "revealed as Val's biological grandmother" (lore-dump §4, flagged "possible scrape artifact").
- Side B: "your fiancé and genealogically your great-grandson" (app/tmp/populate-tara.ts:300, 2026-06-01).
- Canon baseline says "Val is her grandchild AND fiancé" (tara-almswood-lady-death.md).
- Affects: the "Dearest Val" letter, the closed time-loop math, populated Tara seed data.

**C-7. Tara's origin realm — pre-Kether future universe vs Rhea/Tiberoak**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** **Kether is simply what neo-humans call their universe; it is far-future Earth.** Neo-humans harnessed the entire universe and halted entropy. In Jude's earlier era, individual planets just had their own names — "Kether" as a unifying name is a later, post-consolidation term. "Pre-Kether" = same continuity, earlier era, not a separate realm. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7)
- Side A: "He[r] origin story is actually in a future universe of pre Kether just before the creation of neo humans" (Mike, claude-0123, 2025-03-23).
- Side B: "Tara originated from Rhea (in a future universe called Tiberoak)" (claude-0123, same conversation, AI summary of Mike's docs).
- Affects: prequel setting, Tiberoak lore, whether "Rhea" is a place (and its relation to Rhea Calius, see Q-15).
- Possibly reconcilable (Tiberoak/Rhea = the pre-Kether future universe?) — UNKNOWN, needs Michael.

---

### B. Prime Party names & identities

**C-8. Val's canonical name — Pendragon vs Calius vs Duvai'in/Duvai'Tin (+ Elluin)**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Not a contradiction — Val is ancient enough to have accumulated multiple names across eras, each with its own story (Pendragon, Calius, Duvai'in, Elluin, "Magna Volumen"). Current default identity for seed data: **Valmir Calius "Magna Volumen" Duvai'in**; the others are legacy aliases, valid as future lore hooks, not competing errors. **"Duvai'Tin" is a misspelling of Duvai'in — struck as a variant.** **"Elluin" — context unknown, stays [OPEN], not dropped.** (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1)
- Side A: "Valmir Calius (who became the God of Progress)" (claude-0164, 2025-04-01; Mike affirms "yes it is Valmir for sure"); GROWTH-DESIGN-TRUTH §15 "Valmir Calius (Progress)".
- Side B: "Valmir Elluin Duvai'in ... House Duvai'in" (5e sheet, Core Rulebook v0.4.0); "Valmir Duvai'Tin" (GROWTH__Tarot_for_GROWTH.docx).
- Side C: "Val Pendragon" (memory: val-pendragon-character-voice-2025-03-30; app/scripts/seed-godheads.ts:220,223; stt-vocabulary.ts:34).
- Seeded reconciliation: 'Valmir Calius "Magna Volumen" Duvai\'in' (seed-godheads-prime-additions.ts:37) — merges Calius + Duvai'in but drops Pendragon and Elluin.
- Affects: seed data, STT vocabulary, every Val reference in the map; Edmund Duvai'Tin (Emperor) + Rhea Calius (Empress) in the Tarot suggest two family names Valmir bridges.
- Likely resolved by canon roster (Calius + Duvai'in double surname) — but where does "Pendragon" fit (alias? title? error?), and is Elluin vs "Magna Volumen" a middle-name change or two different things? Needs Michael.

**C-9. Trayman — one-third of Triu vs the Demiurge vs original-party member vs Kai's uncle**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** One person across all roles: original mortal party member → mastered Lucidity (did **not** install it — Ma'lo/the Demiurge did) → became one-third of Triu (Three-in-One) → Kai's uncle (Mina's brother). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1)
- Side A: "the original party: Val, Trayman, Et'herling, Thomas, Tara, JEWL" (claude-0027, 2024-11-10); GROWTH-DESIGN-TRUTH §15 lists "Trayman (pattern/history)" as a Prime-Campaign Godhead.
- Side B: Trayman/Selva/Triu are "different incarnations of the same soul package" (claude-0060 era, batch-12, 2024); canon roster: "Triu / Sylva / Trayman — Three-in-One, Watcher of the Terminal."
- Side C: "a virus the Demiurge (Trayman) originally installed" (prime-party-roster.md).
- Side D: "Mina is Kai's mother and Trayman's sister" — Trayman Unfurth, Kai's uncle (GROWTH__Campaign_Notes__Untitled_document.docx).
- Affects: Triu's seeded identity, Kai's family tree, Demiurge lore (C-1), the rulebook's four marginalia voices.
- Canon baseline itself flags this "irreconcilable as written — needs Michael."

**C-10. Original party roster vs current Prime Party**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Current Prime Party, as it stands: **Val, Et'herling, Thomas, JEWL, Tara, Triu, Kai** ("Tailor" = Thomas, name variant). **JEWL is confirmed a party member** (closes the old open question of whether he ever was). **Triu is "separate but same"** — Trayman, Selva, and Triu remain distinct individuals while also functioning as one unified Three-in-One; both framings are simultaneously true, not contradictory. Note: "party" is used loosely — these are cosmic beings mostly pursuing their own agendas, not a tight adventuring group. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §9)
- Side A: "Formation of the party (Transients): Et'herling, Tara, Aiden, Sara, Tailor, Trayman" (claude-0146, 2025-03-29, AI summary Mike solicited).
- Side B: "Our godheads consist of characters like Tara, Trayman, Val, Et'herling, ect." (Mike, claude-0058, 2024-12-06); "the original party: Val, Trayman, Et'herling, Thomas, Tara, JEWL" (claude-0027, 2024-11-10).
- Side C: canonical 6 = Val, Tara, Kai, Et'herling, Triu, Thomas (prime-party-roster.md).
- Affects: who ascended; whether "Transients" is the canonical mortal-era party name; the fates of Aiden/Sara/Tailor/Trayman; whether JEWL was ever a party member.
- [inferred] mortal-era campaign party vs ascended 2026 roster — but the mapping (Trayman→Triu? Tailor→Thomas?) is unconfirmed. Needs Michael.

**C-11. Kai's gender and title**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Kai is **she/her**; title is **"Goddess of Chaos and Balance"** (not "Order"). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1)
- Side A: "Kai The Goddess of Chaos" ("The End", undated); "Kai's Domain will have evolved with an elegance she would have appreciated" (Core Rulebook v0.3.6, Triu's line — antecedent of "she" ambiguous); "Kai Kesdeja... she... goddess of chaos and order" (claude-0084, 2025-02-02); Kai CS uses "her" contract language ("requiring her to create another").
- Side B: memory kai-history-and-family treats Kai as male-coded ("lost his arms"; "JEWL father in name, Bart biological, Mina mother").
- Title variants: "God-head of Chaos and Balance" (seed-godheads.ts:77) vs "Chaos and order" (Mike, chatgpt-0935, 2025-03-24) vs "Goddess of Chaos" ("The End").
- Affects: Kai's seed prompt, pronouns everywhere, the Triu "she would have appreciated" line (see Q-16 cluster).
- Needs Michael: gender/pronouns, and Balance vs Order in the title.

**C-12. Et'herling — Justice vs Mediation; pillar Mercy vs Balance**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Goddess of **Mediation**, pillar **Mercy** (not Justice, not Balance). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7)
- Side A: "God-head of Justice… router of divine will" (seed-godheads.ts:121-127); GROWTH-DESIGN-TRUTH §15 "Et'herling (Justice)".
- Side B: "Goddess of Mediation," pillar MERCY, earned via Forseti's trolley-problem test (prime-party-roster.md: "Early lore said 'Justice'; canonical role here = Mediation").
- Side C: "Et'herling oversees MERCY" while her own pillar is BALANCE (seed-godheads-secondary.ts:177 — file hedges "the cosmology of these primaries can shift").
- Affects: seeded godhead prompts (currently stale), Forge chain framing, pantheon assignments.
- Likely resolved by canon: Mediation, pillar MERCY — confirm and fix the seeds.

**C-13. Trayman vs Roy — which is Spirit, which is Soul**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** **Trayman = Body, Selva = Spirit, Triu = Soul.** Roy was **never** part of this three — that structure is superseded (consistent with Roy being confirmed destroyed/gone, Session Corrections §6). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7)
- Mike verbatim, self-unresolved: "the base manual is the body, Trayman is like the Spirit, and Roy is the Soul, or is it trayman is the soul, and roy is the spirit, Idk but you see it?" (claude-0005, 2024-11-08).
- Post-swap wrinkle: if Roy = "essentially the Soul" and Trayman = "essentially the Spirit" (Nov 2024, pre-swap labels), do their roles swap with the Jan-2026 label swap or keep their names' meanings?
- Affects: the rulebook's three-layer voice structure (base manual / Trayman / Roy).

**C-14. Roy — Godhead "observer" vs Outside-tier adversary**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Roy was **never formally one of the seated Godheads.** His relationship to the party evolved in three stages: perceived as a strange friend at first → then as an enemy → and finally, at his death, the party learned his true nature (bred Demiurge-conduit who outgrew his controller and orchestrated Ma'lo's expulsion, per Session Corrections §6). He worked adjacent to/through the party across that arc rather than as a member of it. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §9)
- Side A: GROWTH-DESIGN-TRUTH §15: "Roy (the observer)" — listed among Prime-Campaign Godheads.
- Side B: Roy = "independent entity," Outside-tier, creator of Alkahest; "Roy Unchained" is the boss fight that killed Kai (memory: prime-cosmology-terms.md).
- Affects: everything Roy-related — he is the single largest open-question cluster in the corpus (see Q-1..Q-4).

**C-15. Tara treated as separate from Lady Death (AI drift, uncorrected)**
- **✅ RULED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Confirmed already-resolved — one Godhead, two names. The "separate beings" version was AI drift, not canon. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §7)
- Side A: "Lady Death will soon notice the anomaly and may take more direct action to investigate or counteract Tara's influence" (AI, chatgpt-1130, 2025-05-21 — two beings; Mike did not correct it).
- Side B: canon: "Lady Death **is** Tara Almswood (one Godhead, two names)" (00_CANON_CORE §6).
- Related: 2016 Dunden's Manor notes show Tara as a normal human participant near Garlo — canon says she "became Death organically through narrative" (GROWTH-DESIGN-TRUTH §15), and the modern-Earth Tara.docx (15yo on a school bus) is flagged "almost certainly a literary rewrite, not a retcon" (prime-cosmology-terms.md).
- Affects: nothing if confirmed — resolved by canon; listed so the 2025 chat and the 2016/2024 variants are formally marked superseded/rewrite.
