### C. Pillars, Soul/Spirit & symbol systems

**C-16. The Soul/Spirit label swap (blanket entry — resolved, listed for the record)**
- Side A (representative, pre-swap): "🜍 Sulfur (Soul) Flow… Frequency… Focus… ☿ Mercury (Spirit) Will - Wisdom - Wit" (Mike-dictated, chatgpt-0085, 2024-01-26); "flow frequency and focus are soul attributes and wisdom wit and willpower are spirit" (Mike verbatim, chatgpt-0106, 2024-07-30); Prequel.docx: "this Mercury is the plant's spirit. Not to be confused with its soul, also called 'Sulfur'".
- Side B (canon, Jan-2026, SETTLED): Spirit = Sulfur = Flow/Frequency/Focus (Purple #582a72); Soul = Mercury = Willpower/Wisdom/Wit (Blue #002f6c) (00_CANON_CORE §2).
- Affects: reading EVERY pre-2026 document — all lore quoted from them must be label-translated. Echoed in ≥14 batches (03, 07, 11, 12, 14, 15, 16, 17, 18, 19, 26, 28, 31, 34, 35).
- Resolved by canon ("SETTLED, do not re-litigate"). One residual to verify: Mike's 2024 dictation attached cosmological freight to the pre-swap labels ("Soul as purest form... Body < Soul > Spirit chevron with Frequency at center") — did that freight move with the labels? (chatgpt-0106/v0.3.7, batch-18.)

**C-17. Stale swap-paragraph colors in CURRENT docs (live doc bug)**
- Side A: CLAUDE.md swap paragraph: "actually **Spirit** (Sulfur/Blue)... actually **Soul** (Mercury/Purple)"; 00_CANON_CORE §1 name-styling: "W/T/H=Spirit(blue)... governed by Soul(purple)".
- Side B: the settled palette in the SAME docs: Spirit=Purple #582a72 (Daath), Soul=Blue #002f6c (Chokmah) (00_CANON_CORE §2; claude-0378, 2026-01-23: "Purple = Spirit (not Soul), Blue = Soul (not Spirit)").
- Affects: agents keep re-tripping on this; two authoritative files contradict themselves internally.
- Likely resolved by canon §2 (Spirit=Purple, Soul=Blue) — confirm so the parentheticals can be silently fixed (per soul-spirit-colors-settled memory: "fix stale docs silently").

**C-18. "Soul Package" vs "Spirit Package" — name AND contents post-swap**
- Side A: "Soul attributes remain in package (Focus, Flow)" (claude-0010, 2024-11-08, pre-swap — those attributes are now SPIRIT).
- Side B: "The 'Soul Package' terminology might still be correct from the game's naming perspective even if the pillar labels changed... maybe it should be 'Spirit Package' now?" (claude-0381, 2026-02-05 — unresolved).
- Canon §6 resolves the MECHANICS: on death Spirit is kept unchanged (incl. all 10 magic schools), Soul halved (lost half → Lady Death), Frequency KRMA → Lady Death, Body → GM. The NAME of the persistent package is still open (00_CANON_CORE §11 lists "Spirit/Soul Package composition detail" as NEEDS MIKE).
- Affects: death-engine UI, GDT §13 "Soul Packages as licensable ML-agent IP," Lady Death lore ("Frequency transferred to Lady Death").

**C-19. W/T/H gates ↔ pillars mapping (post-swap unresolved)**
- Side A: "wealth - Spirit, Tech - Soul, Health - Body" (chatgpt-1417, 2025-08-20, same-day search).
- Side B: "Wealth = Body... Health = Spirit... Tech = Soul" (AI mapping unchallenged by Mike, 2025-08-28).
- Also same file: "O is opportunity and it ties directly to wealth. tech is resistance" (Mike's GRO-facet↔gate mirror, chatgpt-1417, 2025-08-20).
- Affects: the name-level symbolism of GRO.WTH itself (canon §1 has G/R/O=Body, W/T/H=Spirit as a block, but no per-letter gate↔pillar map), Thread system design.
- Both pre-swap and both mid-search; final harmonization UNKNOWN — needs Michael.

**C-20. GRO.WTH acronym letters**
- Side A: "growth actually stands for Goals, resistance, opportunity, wealth, tech, and health" (Mike verbatim, claude-0334, 2025-08-21 — "This is the most recent development").
- Side B: "gro.vines with goals opposition and opportunity" (Mike, chatgpt-1427, 2025-08-23 — Opposition, two days later).

- Affects: the name of the game; memory says the acronym was "corrected" again later (growth-acronym-corrected) — state the final letters once, for the record.

**C-21. Severity/Balance/Mercy — pillar-level triad, intra-pillar polarity, or pantheon axis?**
- Side A: "The **three pillars** (Severity, Balance, Mercy)... correspond to the **Body, Spirit, and Soul** structure" (chatgpt-0738, 2025-02-10, AI-restated).
- Side B: intra-pillar polarity: "Focus (Severity)... Flow (Mercy)" (claude-0378, 2026-01-23, AI recap of then-current docs).

- Affects: magic system framing, pantheon lore, whether the triad is fractal (appearing at every scale) by design.
- Likely resolved by canon at two scales already — confirm whether the Body/Spirit/Soul-correspondence reading (side A) is also true or dead.

**C-22. Gender polarity of Body/Soul/Spirit (Mike self-contradiction, flagged fractal)**
- Side A: "we have body, soul, spirit... Clasical mystiscm. Female, balance, male." (Mike, chatgpt-1248, 2025-07-06).
- Side B, moments later: "Masculine is the doing, female is the recieving" + "Body is doing, soul is being, spirit is receiving" → Body=masculine-functioning.
- Mike's own hint: "I didn't even intend to reverse it. Imo it isn't reversed this is a how I absorbed the same mystiscm... because it's a fractal."
- Affects: symbolic layer of the pillars; whether polarity should be canonized fixed or role-relative.

**C-23. Magic school → pillar assignments (Alteration/Fortune swap; Enchantment; Abjuration)**
- Side A (Mike verbatim): "Mercy: Fortune, Restoration, Enchantment. Balance: Divination, Dissolution, Abjuration, Illusion. Severity: Alteration, Conjuration, Force." (chatgpt-1786, 2024-01-25).
- Side B: "Mercy: Alteration, Restoration, Enchantment / Severity: Fortune, Force, Conjuration" (AI-generated ToC, chatgpt-1804, 2024-08-05 — [AI-proposed/possibly AI error], uncorrected).
- Side C: Tara CS 6.0 puts Enchantment under Mercy and Abjuration under Balance; GROWTH v2 brainstorm puts Enchantment under Severity and Abjuration under Mercy.
- Affects: all 10 magic-school docs and the three magic pillars.
- Likely resolved by canon: 00_CANON_CORE §8 = Mercy: Fortune/Restoration/Enchantment; Severity: Force/Alteration/Conjuration; Balance: Divination/Dissolution/Abjuration/Illusion — identical to Mike's 2024-01-25 statement. Confirm; sides B/C are drift.

### Appendix: dated evolutions & rejections (no ruling needed — recorded so nobody re-opens them)

- **Values/Addictions** era statements (2025-07 pitch language, FHRG-KRMA-flow, chatgpt-1501 "in development") — CUT 2026-04-19; **Fears** post-release only. All older mentions superseded.
- **WTH levels** and the 10-level **weight** abstraction — removed (r-2026-04-22-03; weight = actual lbs).
- **KL (Karmic Level)** → **KV/TKV + KRMA** — pure terminology evolution 2024→2025; "KL as character power level" has no 2026 equivalent by design.
- **GM role naming:** Godhead (2025-02) → Watcher; GODHEAD reassigned to the AI-agent tier (current CLAUDE.md hierarchy). [inferred sequence, uncontested]
- **Nature-reclaims-civilization setting** (AI deep-research GDD, chatgpt-0989, 2025-04-12) — REJECTED by Mike ("that is unfourtunate"); GROWTH is multi-genre/multi-era. Not canon; do not reuse.
- **Sephirot location:** seeded under Tree of Life (tmp/seed-tree-of-life-rooms.ts), then deliberately re-parented into the Terminal tower (fix-sephirot-terminal-and-prime-dupe.ts) — matches r-2026-06-11-03. Terminal wins.
- **Pre-swap "Body (Red), Soul (Purple), Spirit (Blue)"** statements (2025-04-13, 2025-04-30, 2025-08-06, SDD, Tarot, etc.) — all dated pre-swap labeling; colors stayed with the triads, labels swapped (see C-16).
- **Ma'lo "mentor vs Demiurge"** — same character: Tara's exorcist/alchemy mentor who became the final antagonist; Demiurge-tier from session one (1/9/2016 body-jump log; prime-campaign-endgame-mythos). Not a contradiction.
- **Kai's parentage** — resolved by memory: "JEWL father in name, Bart biological, Mina mother" (kai-history-and-family) — both lore-dump variants were partial truths.

**Entry count: 41 contradictions + 9 recorded evolutions/rejections.**

## OPEN QUESTIONS / HOLES

> ~200 raw questions from ~40 extraction batches, deduplicated to the genuinely open ones. Every entry is a direct question to Michael. Questions the current canon baseline already answers were dropped — see the appendix at the bottom for those, with citations. Where a question overlaps a numbered contradiction, the C-number is referenced instead of repeating it.

---

### A. Prime Party & core characters

**Roy** (the single most-asked hole in the corpus — asked in 12+ batches):
- **Q-1. Who is Roy?** He appears as: GDT's Prime-Campaign Godhead "the observer"; the Outside-tier creator of Alkahest whose "Roy Unchained" form killed Kai; an NYPD augmenter in campaign lore; one of the four rulebook marginalia voices; Kai's sworn enemy ("the tools" to destroy him); "nerd boy" in the Boys Campaign; Elmer Cain's protectee; tied to "the author's personal journey." Which of these are one being, and what is his full identity, role, and fate? (cf. C-14)
  - **✅ ANSWERED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Roy = **an occultist who started in New York → demon hunter/exorcist → plane-walking Lucid wizard = "The Chalk Magician"** (the cross-era comic-book legend); a **conduit bred by Ma'lo/the Demiurge** who grew too capable ("giving Ma'lo a run for his money"), set the scheme that ultimately expelled the Demiurge, and assembled the perfect party via **The Four** (its true purpose). **Never formally a seated Godhead** — perceived as strange friend → enemy → true nature learned at his death; **destroyed at the end (presumed, not confirmed)**. The "nerd boy" appearance falls with the struck Boys Campaign. (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §6, §9, §2)
- **Q-2.** In Roy's rulebook line "It is a simple quarter turn from fear to love, That's why it's so easy for him to control" — who is "him"? The Demiurge? (v0.3.6/0.3.7 marginalia)
- **Q-3.** What is Roy's "solution" that Tara weighs in her End-CS goal ("Perhaps Roy is right, but there must be an alternative to his solution")?
- **Q-4.** Are multiple Roy instances canon? ("each roy is a human that is in transit"; "Roys observing the entrance" at the Tree of Life.) And what is the "Roy operator symbol" at the center of the game emblem (Ouroboros + 3 triangles)?
- **Q-5.** Is Roy the ROY G BIV / color-spectrum entity Claude once guessed, or something else entirely? (You never confirmed — chatgpt-era, batch-14.)

**Trayman / Triu / Selva:**
- **Q-6. Who is Trayman, finally?** One-third of Triu/Sylva/Trayman, the Demiurge, Kai's uncle (Trayman Unfurth, Mina's brother), an original-party member, a rulebook voice, "the original writer losing touch with his own singularity" — which of these hold, and what is his final arc/fate? (cf. C-1, C-9)
  - **✅ ANSWERED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** one person across all roles — original mortal party member → mastered Lucidity (did NOT install it; Ma'lo/the Demiurge did) → became one-third of Triu → Kai's uncle (Mina's brother). Also: obtained Lucidity and was **groomed as Roy's replacement conduit**. He is NOT the Demiurge (that is Ma'lo, C-1). (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §1, §6)
- **Q-7.** What was Triu before Lucidity? Whose soul package do the Trayman/Selva/Triu incarnations share, and what is the gender/identity across incarnations (Triu is tagged HERstory)?
  - **✅ PARTIALLY ANSWERED 2026-07-09 [LOCKED]:** Triu is "separate but same" — Trayman, Selva, and Triu remain distinct individuals while also functioning as one unified Three-in-One; both framings simultaneously true. ## Struck From Canon (ruled 2026-07-09)

Per Michael's correction pass (Session Corrections 2026-07-09, §2). Each item was removed/annotated in the Roster, Relationships, Factions, and Timeline entries above and is recorded here for the permanent record:

1. **"Boys Campaign" + the character Arubella** — NOT canon; struck entirely. (Reason: Michael ruled the campaign and the character non-canon.) Roster table row, player-map entry (Bryden→Arubella), campaign tables, and NPC-notes bullet annotated/removed above; Karen Almswood's status falls with it pending a separate ruling.
2. **Argentum Sanguis as Prime-Campaign content** — confirmed NOT part of the Prime Campaign. (Reason: side content, different setting.) The rulebook easter-egg entry stands, annotated.
3. **Tristan Gifford as a fictional Moroi PC in "The Ones Who Drain"** — struck. (Reason: mis-attribution — Tristan Gifford is a real person: Michael's co-creator, played Val, DMed the 5e side-campaign. Only the fictional-PC attribution is struck; he remains in the real-world-people group.)
4. **"Valmir + Mina → son Amon→Tyre"** — struck as incorrect. (Reason: one Mina; she is Kai's mother, not Tyre's mother, and not romantically involved with Val; Tyre *turned* Mina into a Moroi. Tyre remains Val's son; his mother is [OPEN] → Q-136.)
